## UI Components

- [Aceternity UI](https://ui.aceternity.com/) - Aceternity UI is a free collection of animated UI components, effects, and blocks built with React, Tailwind CSS, and Motion (Framer Motion's successor). Rather than a traditional installable library, it provides copy-paste code snippets that developers directly integrate into their projects. It features hero sections, bento grids, 3D card effects, animated backgrounds, and many more visually striking components designed for modern web interfaces.

• Offers 1000+ animated components, blocks, and effects
• Powered by Tailwind CSS and Motion for smooth animations
• Copy-paste architecture — no dependency on the library at runtime
• Components are fully customizable after integration

Primary use cases include SaaS landing pages, startup websites, portfolios, and marketing sites that need premium-quality animations and visual polish. Compared to shadcn/ui (which focuses on accessible, unstyled primitives) or Tailwind UI (which is a paid product), Aceternity UI is entirely free and prioritizes eye-catching motion and visual impact over component completeness. ([Read more](/details/aceternity-ui.md)) `Animation` `Framer Motion` `Tailwind`
- [Apex](https://dashboardpack.com/theme-details/apex-dashboard-nextjs/) - Comprehensive React admin dashboard built with Next.js 16 and shadcn/ui, featuring 125+ static routes across five dashboard variants including Overview, Analytics, eCommerce, CRM, and SaaS. Includes a live theme customizer, authentication with 2FA, Command Palette, and i18n support. ([Read more](/details/apex.md)) `React` `Next.js` `Shadcn Ui`
- [cmdk](https://cmdk.paco.me) - Fast, unstyled command menu React component (⌘K) with no dependencies. Features fuzzy search, keyboard navigation, and nested commands for building custom command palettes. ([Read more](/details/cmdk.md)) `Headless` `Command Palette` `Keyboard Shortcuts`
- [Heroicons](https://heroicons.com/) - Heroicons is a beautiful, hand-crafted set of over 290 SVG icon components created by the makers of Tailwind CSS, available in both outline and solid styles with full TypeScript support and native React integration. Designed on a 24x24 pixel grid with meticulous attention to visual consistency, it delivers icons that integrate seamlessly into any Tailwind-based or standalone React application. Key features include dual style variants (outline and solid) for every icon, native React components with full TypeScript definitions, three sizing options (16px, 20px, 24px), seamless integration with Tailwind CSS utility classes for coloring and sizing, MIT licensing for unrestricted commercial use, and exceptional bundle performance with a Delta/Source(gzip) ratio close to 1.0x–1.2x. Primary use cases include navigation icons, button icons, status indicators, form field icons, and any React application requiring polished, consistent iconography. Compared to larger icon libraries like FontAwesome (heavier, less consistent with Tailwind aesthetics) or Material Icons (Google-specific design language), Heroicons offers the best visual match for Tailwind-based projects with minimal overhead. ([Read more](/details/heroicons.md)) `Icons` `Svg` `Tailwind Css`
- [Masonic](https://github.com/jaredLunde/masonic) - High-performance React masonry component with virtualization. Efficiently renders tens of thousands of grid cells without lag using advanced algorithms. ([Read more](/details/masonic.md)) `Masonry` `Virtualization` `Performance`
- [Planby](https://planby.app/) - React component for building schedules, timelines, and electronic program guides (EPG) for TV, VOD, music events, and more. Lightweight, customizable, and trusted by 100+ companies. ([Read more](/details/planby.md)) `Scheduler` `Timeline` `Epg`
- [React Aria](https://react-aria.adobe.com) - Comprehensive collection of unstyled, accessible React hooks for building components with full keyboard navigation, screen reader support, and ARIA attributes built-in. Provides the foundation for accessible UI libraries. ([Read more](/details/react-aria.md)) `Accessibility` `Hooks` `Unstyled`
- [React Beautiful DnD](https://github.com/atlassian/react-beautiful-dnd) - Accessible drag-and-drop library for React with beautiful animations and physics. Provides accessible drag-and-drop functionality with support for keyboard navigation and accessibility features. ([Read more](/details/react-beautiful-dnd.md)) `Drag Drop` `Accessible` `Animation`
- [React Code Highlighter](https://github.com/react-syntax-highlighter/react-syntax-highlighter) - React Syntax Highlighter is a comprehensive syntax highlighting component built on prism.js and highlight.js that displays over 200 programming languages with 40+ visual themes in React applications. It is currently the largest React code highlighting library with 4000+ GitHub stars and 250K+ weekly npm downloads. Key features include support for 180+ languages via prism.js and 50+ via highlight.js, line numbers and line highlighting for code documentation, multiple visual themes optimized for light and dark mode, copy-to-clipboard integration, custom component overriding for tokens, and lazy loading support for large code blocks. Primary use cases include developer documentation sites, code playground platforms, technical blogs, API documentation, tutorial platforms, and developer tools requiring syntax-highlighted code display. Compared to lighter alternatives like react-shiki (which uses Shiki for VS Code-quality highlighting but has a larger bundle), or react-code-blocks (fewer themes and less community adoption), React Syntax Highlighter offers the widest language and theme support with the largest ecosystem. ([Read more](/details/react-code-highlighter.md)) `Open Source` `Code Display` `Syntax Highlighting`
- [React Countdown Circle Timer](https://github.com/vydimitrov/react-countdown-circle-timer) - Lightweight circular countdown timer with color transitions and smooth animations. Perfect for timed quizzes, workout intervals, and visual time displays. ([Read more](/details/react-countdown-circle-timer.md)) `Countdown` `Circular` `Animation`
- [React Flow](https://reactflow.dev/) - React Flow (also known as React Flow by xyflow) is a highly customizable node-based UI library for building interactive flow diagrams, node editors, and visual programming interfaces in React applications. It provides an intuitive API for creating connected node graphs with drag-and-drop, zoom, and pan capabilities. Key features include a performant canvas-based rendering engine supporting thousands of nodes, built-in minimap and controls for navigation, customizable node and edge types with React components, undo/redo history management, and support for both controlled and uncontrolled state. Primary use cases include workflow builders, data pipeline editors, visual programming tools, mind mapping applications, and any interface requiring interactive node-and-connection diagrams. Compared to alternatives like Flowchart.js (limited customization) or building custom D3-based node editors, React Flow provides a production-ready solution with React integration, extensive customization hooks, and active commercial backing from xyflow. ([Read more](/details/react-flow.md)) `Open Source` `Node Editor` `Flow Visualization`
- [React Grid Layout](https://github.com/react-grid-layout/react-grid-layout) - Draggable and resizable grid layout system for React. Build dashboard-style interfaces with drag-and-drop, responsive breakpoints, and persistent layouts. ([Read more](/details/react-grid-layout.md)) `Grid` `Drag Drop` `Layout`
- [React Icons](https://github.com/react-icons/react-icons) - React Icons is the largest SVG icon library for React with over 10,000 icons from 20+ popular icon sets including Font Awesome, Material Design Icons, Lucide, Heroicons, Tabler Icons, Devicons, and more. It uses ES6 import syntax with tree-shaking support so you only bundle the icons you actually use, keeping your bundle size minimal. Key features include 20+ icon packages with 10,000+ total icons from sources like Font Awesome 5/6, Material Design Icons, Lucide, Heroicons, Tabler, Phosphor, Boxicons, and Devicons, full tree-shaking support ensuring zero-cost imports for unused icons, native SVG rendering with no external font dependencies, customizable sizing and coloring via standard React props and CSS, TypeScript support with auto-generated type definitions for all icons, and a simple unified import API across all icon sets. Primary use cases include navigation icons, button icons, status indicators, form field icons, sidebar navigation, and any React application requiring polished, scalable iconography. Compared to using raw SVG files from individual libraries (which requires managing multiple imports and inconsistent APIs) or icon font solutions like FontAwesome (which add larger font files), React Icons provides a unified, tree-shakeable API for accessing the entire icon ecosystem from a single package. ([Read more](/details/react-icons.md)) `Open Source` `Icons` `Svg`
- [React Resizable Panels](https://react-resizable-panels.vercel.app) - Resizable panel groups for React with horizontal and vertical layouts, collapsible panels, and persistence support. Built by the creator of React DevTools. ([Read more](/details/react-resizable-panels.md)) `Layout` `Resizable` `Panels`
- [React Shepherd](https://react-shepherd.vercel.app) - React wrapper for Shepherd.js tour library with Popper.js positioning. Create guided tours with responsive overlay dialogs in under 20 lines of code. ([Read more](/details/react-shepherd.md)) `Tour Guides` `Onboarding` `Shepherd`
- [Reactour](https://docs.react.tours) - Popular guided product tour library with 3.3k GitHub stars. Features modular packages for tours, masks, and popovers to highlight and explain app features. ([Read more](/details/reactour.md)) `Tour Guides` `Onboarding` `Walkthroughs`
- [@anatoliygatt/heart-switch](https://github.com/anatoliygatt/heart-switch) - @anatoliygatt/heart-switch is a lightweight React toggle switch component with an animated heart-shaped design for a unique, visually appealing UI element. Built with full accessibility support including ARIA attributes and keyboard navigation, it works seamlessly in any React application. Key features include a smooth sliding animation, customizable colors via props, TypeScript support, and a minimal footprint with zero runtime dependencies. Primary use cases include adding playful, themed toggles to settings pages, profile editors, and preference panels. Compared to standard toggle switches, this offers a distinctive heart-themed design that stands out, while maintaining the same accessibility standards expected from production-ready components. ([Read more](/details/anatoliygattheart-switch.md)) `Toggle` `Accessible` `Heart Shaped`
- [@anatoliygatt/numeric-stepper](https://github.com/anatoliygatt/numeric-stepper) - @anatoliygatt/numeric-stepper is a lightweight React component that provides accessible increment/decrement controls for numeric input values. Built with full keyboard navigation support, ARIA attributes, and configurable min/max bounds, it offers a polished alternative to bare HTML number inputs. Key features include configurable step sizes, custom styling through props, TypeScript support, and a minimal zero-dependency footprint. Primary use cases include quantity selectors in e-commerce carts, setting controls in dashboards, form number inputs, and configuration panels. Compared to raw HTML number inputs (which have inconsistent cross-browser styling and accessibility), this component provides a consistent, themeable, and accessible UI across all browsers. ([Read more](/details/anatoliygattnumeric-stepper.md)) `Numeric Input` `Accessible` `Themeable`
- [Achromatic Color Picker](https://achromatic.dev/docs/components/color-picker) - Achromatic Color Picker is a lightweight, zero-dependency color picker component built for React and Next.js applications using Tailwind CSS and shadcn/ui conventions. It provides essential color selection capabilities including hue and alpha sliders, hex/RGB/HSL input fields, and browser eyedropper API integration without pulling in any external libraries.

• Zero external dependencies for minimal bundle impact
• Hue slider, alpha/channel transparency control, and eyedropper tool
• Direct hex, RGB, and HSL color input fields
• Fully themable through Tailwind CSS and shadcn/ui conventions

Primary use cases include theme configuration panels, design system tools, and brand color customization interfaces in dashboards and admin panels. Compared to heavier alternatives like react-color (which can add significant bundle size) or Chrome picker libraries, Achromatic Color Picker achieves the same core functionality with a fraction of the dependencies and bundle weight. ([Read more](/details/achromatic-color-picker.md)) `Color Picker` `Dependency Free` `Shadcn Compatible`
- [Aesthetic](https://github.com/milesj/aesthetic) - Aesthetic is a type-safe, framework-agnostic CSS-in-JS styling library that provides a flexible styling system for JavaScript applications with first-class TypeScript support throughout. It supports multiple styling paradigms including plain JavaScript object styles, stylesheet imports, and external class name references while generating atomic CSS for optimal runtime performance. Key features include framework-agnostic API compatible with React, Vue, Angular, and vanilla JS, atomic CSS generation for minimal bundle size, server-side rendering support out of the box, theme management with CSS custom properties, and comprehensive TypeScript type inference for all style objects. Primary use cases include component library foundations, design system implementations, and multi-framework projects where type safety and performance are priorities. Compared to styled-components or Emotion (which are React-centric and generate duplicate CSS at runtime), Aesthetic offers broader framework support with stronger TypeScript integration and more efficient atomic CSS output, though it has a smaller community and fewer integrations. ([Read more](/details/aesthetic.md)) `Css In Js` `Type Safe` `Framework Agnostic`
- [Ant Design](https://ant.design) - Ant Design is a comprehensive enterprise-level UI component library for React, featuring 80+ production-ready components built on a consistent design language. Developed by Ant Group, it provides everything needed to build complex business applications including data tables, forms, navigation, and feedback components. Key features include internationalization for 100+ languages, built-in accessibility with ARIA support, responsive grid system, dark mode theming, and TypeScript-first development. Primary use cases include enterprise dashboards, admin panels, SaaS applications, and internal business tools. Compared to alternatives like Material-UI (which follows Google's Material Design), Ant Design has a more enterprise-focused aesthetic with advanced data components like tree selects, cascading selects, and configurable tables. ([Read more](/details/ant-design.md)) `Open Source` `Enterprise Grade` `Internationalization`
- [Ant Design Pro](https://pro.ant.design) - Ant Design Pro is a production-ready React admin framework developed by Alibaba's Ant Design team, providing a comprehensive out-of-the-box solution for building enterprise administrative interfaces. It includes over 20 pre-built business pages, an integrated ProComponents library for rapid form and table development, and full TypeScript support throughout the codebase. Key features include route-level access control, built-in internationalization with support for 15+ languages, integration with UmiJS build tooling, and enterprise-grade design quality tested at massive scale. Primary use cases include admin dashboards, CRM systems, content management platforms, and internal enterprise tools requiring polished, production-ready UI. Compared to simpler admin templates like React Admin or custom-built admin panels, Ant Design Pro offers a more comprehensive, opinionated framework with stronger defaults and Alibaba-scale proven reliability, though it has a steeper learning curve. ([Read more](/details/ant-design-pro.md)) `Admin Dashboard` `Enterprise` `Typescript`
- [Berry MUI React](https://berrydashboard.io/free/) - Material UI dashboard with a distinctive color palette and bold styling by CodedThemes, featuring dark/light modes, authentication pages, ApexCharts integration, Redux state management, and nine demo pages. ([Read more](/details/berry-mui-react.md)) `Material Design` `Dashboard` `Auth`
- [Blueprint UI](https://blueprintjs.com) - Blueprint UI is a comprehensive React-based UI toolkit designed primarily for complex, data-dense desktop applications. Developed by Palantir, it provides over 50 components including data tables, date pickers, tree views, and form controls optimized for business workflows. Key features include built-in dark mode, keyboard accessibility, TypeScript-first design, and extensive customization through CSS variables and component props. Primary use cases include data-intensive dashboards, financial applications, analytics platforms, and enterprise internal tools. Compared to lighter libraries like Chakra UI, Blueprint prioritizes data-heavy components and productivity workflows over marketing UI patterns. ([Read more](/details/blueprint-ui.md)) `Blueprint` `Open Source` `React`
- [Captcha Image](https://github.com/tpkahlon/captcha-image) - Captcha Image is a lightweight JavaScript library that generates random CAPTCHA images for human verification in web forms. It renders CAPTCHA text as distorted images with configurable noise, colors, and character settings to prevent automated bot submissions without requiring external services.

**Key Features:**
- Random CAPTCHA image generation using Canvas API
- Configurable character sets, length, and font styles
- Adjustable noise, distortion, and background colors
- Zero external dependencies and server calls
- Simple API with validation callback
- Framework-agnostic usage with React integration examples

**Primary Use Cases:** Registration forms, contact forms, login pages, and comment systems that need lightweight bot protection without relying on third-party services like reCAPTCHA.

**Compared to Alternatives:** Unlike Google reCAPTCHA (which requires API keys and tracks users), this library is fully self-contained and privacy-friendly. However, it lacks the advanced ML-based security of modern CAPTCHA services. ([Read more](/details/captcha-image.md)) `Captcha` `Security` `Image`
- [Carbon Design System](https://www.carbondesignsystem.com/) - Carbon Design System is IBM's open-source design system providing a comprehensive set of enterprise-grade UI components built on the IBM Design Language. The React implementation offers 80+ components including data tables, forms, navigation, and data visualization widgets optimized for complex enterprise applications. Key features include design token support, dark mode theming, internationalization, WCAG accessibility compliance, and integration with IBM Cloud services. Primary use cases include enterprise dashboards, SaaS platforms, internal tools, and large-scale web applications requiring consistent branding. Compared to community libraries, Carbon benefits from IBM's rigorous design standards and extensive component coverage for data-intensive interfaces. ([Read more](/details/carbon-design-system.md)) `Ibm` `Enterprise` `Design System`
- [ChatUI](https://chatui.io/) - ChatUI is a specialized React component library designed for building conversational user interfaces, chatbots, and messaging applications. Developed by Alibaba's team, it provides optimized components for chat experiences including message bubbles, quick reply buttons, card messages, and input controls.

**Key Features:**
- Specialized chat-specific components (message bubbles, typing indicators, rich card messages)
- Quick reply and suggestion button support
- Customizable themes and branding
- Mobile-first responsive design
- Rich message type support (text, image, video, files, cards)
- Built-in input controls with emoji and attachment support

**Primary Use Cases:** Customer service chatbots, in-app messaging systems, AI assistant interfaces, live chat widgets, and community communication platforms.

**Compared to Alternatives:** Unlike general-purpose UI libraries like Material-UI or Ant Design which require building chat components from scratch, ChatUI provides chat-optimized components out of the box. Compared to Stream Chat or Sendbird (full backend services), ChatUI is purely a frontend UI library without backend services. ([Read more](/details/chatui.md)) `Chat` `Conversational` `Alibaba`
- [colorReact](https://github.com/elrumordelaluz/coloreact) - colorReact is a minimal, ultra-lightweight color picker component for React applications that provides a simple color selection widget with a tiny bundle footprint. It renders an intuitive color selection UI that can be embedded in forms, style editors, or theme customization panels with minimal code.

**Key Features:**
- Ultra-lightweight at just a few kilobytes gzipped
- Simple, intuitive color picking interface
- onChange callback for real-time color updates
- Zero external dependencies
- Easy customization through CSS
- Works seamlessly with React's standard state management patterns

**Primary Use Cases:** Form color inputs, theme configuration panels, brand color selectors, and design customization tools in React applications that need a simple color picker without heavy dependencies.

**Compared to Alternatives:** Unlike react-color (which offers multiple picker styles like Sketch, Chrome, and Photoshop at ~100KB), colorReact focuses on a single minimal pattern with a fraction of the bundle size. It trades advanced features like color format conversion for simplicity and lightweight integration. ([Read more](/details/colorreact.md)) `Color Picker` `Tiny` `Minimal`
- [Doist Reactist](https://github.com/Doist/reactist) - Doist Reactist is a collection of open-source React UI components built with Emotion CSS-in-JS, created by Doist (the company behind Todoist and Twist). With 35+ components ranging from basics like buttons, inputs, and tooltips to complex elements like modals, dropdowns, and date pickers, it provides a cohesive design language for building web applications with zero external dependencies.

**Key Features:**
- 35+ production-ready React components
- Zero runtime dependencies (only peer dependency is React)
- Styled with Emotion CSS-in-JS for dynamic theming
- Clean, minimalist design language
- MIT-licensed and open-source
- Consistent API across all components

**Primary Use Cases:** Teams building productivity tools, web applications needing a clean minimal UI foundation, and developers who want quality components without the overhead of large UI libraries.

**Compared to Alternatives:** Unlike Material-UI (100+ components, heavier) or Bootstrap React (many dependencies), Reactist is intentionally minimal with zero dependencies beyond React. It offers fewer components but each is well-crafted for productivity-focused interfaces. ([Read more](/details/doist-reactist.md)) `Open Source` `React` `Ui`
- [Ember](https://dashboardpack.com/theme-details/ember-dashboard/) - Healthcare-focused React admin dashboard with 50+ pages covering Patient Management, Appointments, Vitals Monitor, Prescriptions, Lab Results, Health Records, Bed Management, Telemedicine, and Billing. Built with Next.js and shadcn/ui, designed specifically for medical workflows. ([Read more](/details/ember.md)) `React` `Next.js` `Healthcare`
- [Flowbite React](https://flowbite-react.com) - Flowbite React is an open-source UI component library built on Tailwind CSS, offering over 30+ ready-to-use React components with dark mode support and seamless integration with modern frameworks like Next.js. It emphasizes accessibility and utility-first design principles. ([Read more](/details/flowbite-react.md)) `Tailwind Css` `Dark Mode` `Utility First`
- [Flux](https://dashboardpack.com/theme-details/flux-dashboard-nextjs/) - Gradient-forward React admin dashboard built for SaaS and startup teams, featuring 64+ pages, five dashboard variants, and Framer Motion animations. Includes over 300 color combinations, RTL support, a Command Palette, and 35 shadcn/ui primitives. ([Read more](/details/flux.md)) `React` `Next.js` `Saas`
- [Formsy Material UI](https://github.com/mbrookes/formsy-material-ui) - A compatibility wrapper that bridges Formsy form validation with Material UI form components, enabling seamless form validation in Material Design interfaces. ([Read more](/details/formsy-material-ui.md)) `Forms` `Material Ui` `Validation`
- [Formsy React Components](https://github.com/twisty/formsy-react-components) - A set of reusable React JS components designed for use within formsy-react forms, providing pre-built form elements with integrated validation support. ([Read more](/details/formsy-react-components.md)) `Forms` `Validation` `Reusable`
- [Fortress](https://dashboardpack.com/theme-details/fortress-dashboard/) - Bloomberg-inspired institutional finance dashboard built for trading desks, risk management teams, and compliance officers. Features 57+ pages with 13 finance-specific pages covering multi-asset trading (Fixed Income, FX, Derivatives), risk analytics, and regulatory compliance monitoring. ([Read more](/details/fortress.md)) `React` `Next.js` `Fintech`
- [Hover.dev](https://hover.dev) - Interactive animated UI component library providing production-ready templates, hero sections, cards, and sections with copy-paste workflow. Built with React, Tailwind CSS, and modern animation techniques for fast implementation. ([Read more](/details/hoverdev.md)) `Animated` `Copy Paste` `Tailwind Css`
- [Interweave](https://github.com/milesj/interweave) - A React library for safely rendering HTML content, filtering attributes, autowrapping text with regex matchers, and rendering emoji characters with built-in security protections. ([Read more](/details/interweave.md)) `Html Rendering` `Security` `Emoji`
- [Interweave Emoji Picker](https://github.com/milesj/interweave/tree/master/packages/emoji-picker) - A React-based emoji picker powered by the Interweave library and Emojibase, providing a rich emoji selection experience with search and categorization. ([Read more](/details/interweave-emoji-picker.md)) `Emoji` `Picker` `Interweave`
- [kbar](https://kbar.vercel.app) - Fast, portable, and extensible command palette for React applications with built-in fuzzy search, keyboard shortcuts, and priority-based command ordering. ([Read more](/details/kbar.md)) `Command Palette` `Keyboard Shortcuts` `Search`
- [Kokonut UI](https://github.com/kokonut-labs/kokonutui) - Kokonut UI is a modern, open-source React component library providing beautifully designed, customizable UI components built with contemporary design principles. It focuses on developer experience with copy-paste installation, clean APIs, and components that blend seamlessly into any application aesthetic.

**Key Features:**
- Free and open-source components under MIT license
- Modern, clean design aesthetics suitable for contemporary web apps
- Copy-paste installation model (components become your own code)
- High customizability through CSS and component props
- Regular updates with new components and improvements
- Community-driven development

**Primary Use Cases:** Modern web applications, SaaS dashboards, portfolio websites, and projects where developers want beautiful defaults they can easily customize rather than a rigid design system.

**Compared to Alternatives:** Similar to Aceternity UI's copy-paste model but with less emphasis on dramatic animations and more focus on clean, functional components. Compared to shadcn/ui, it offers a different design aesthetic and may provide components not found in more mainstream libraries. ([Read more](/details/kokonut-ui.md)) `Free` `Modern` `Customizable`
- [LiveKit Components](https://github.com/livekit/components-js) - Official open-source React components for building real-time voice, video, and messaging features with LiveKit. Includes pre-built UI components for agent sessions and audio visualization. ([Read more](/details/livekit-components-js.md)) `Open Source` `React` `LiveKit` `Real Time`
- [Lucide](https://github.com/lucide-icons/lucide) - A beautiful and consistent open-source icon toolkit made by the community, forked from Feather Icons with expanded icon library and active development. ([Read more](/details/lucide.md)) `Icons` `Svg` `Open Source`
- [Lucide React](https://lucide.dev/guide/packages/lucide-react) - A comprehensive icon library with over 1,500 clean, consistent SVG icons designed on a 24×24 grid, built with ES modules for tree-shaking and optimal bundle size. ([Read more](/details/lucide-react.md)) `Icons` `Svg` `Tree Shakable`
- [Mantis React](https://mantisdashboard.com/free/) - Enterprise-focused MUI dashboard by CodedThemes that blends Material UI components with Ant Design's design philosophy, featuring Redux Toolkit state management, ApexCharts, and thorough TypeScript support. - [Material UI](https://github.com/mui/material-ui) - Material UI (MUI) is the most popular React component library implementing Google's Material Design system with over 150 production-ready components, used by more than 10 million developers worldwide. It provides a comprehensive theming system, robust accessibility patterns, and deep customization capabilities through styled-components and CSS-in-JS APIs. Key features include 150+ battle-tested components covering every common UI pattern, a powerful theming system with CSS variables and createTheme API for light/dark/custom themes, built-in responsive design utilities including useMediaQuery and responsive breakpoints, comprehensive accessibility compliance following WAI-ARIA guidelines, official support for Next.js server components and React Server Components, TypeScript-first API design with complete type definitions, and a rich ecosystem including MUI X (DataGrid, Date Picker, Charts). Primary use cases include enterprise admin dashboards, SaaS applications, internal tools, and any React project needing a polished, Material Design-inspired interface. Compared to alternatives like Ant Design (which offers more components but less Western market adoption) or Chakra UI (more modern aesthetics but smaller ecosystem), MUI offers the largest community, most documentation, and longest track record, though its heavier bundle size and opinionated Material aesthetic may not suit all projects. ([Read more](/details/material-ui.md)) `Material Design` `Component Library` `Open Source`

It implements the classic Kanban pattern for visual workflow management with smooth, accessible drag interactions.

**Key Features:**
- Drag cards between and within columns
- Smooth, physics-based drag animations via react-beautiful-dnd
- Column management (add, remove, reorder)
- Card CRUD operations within the board
- Keyboard-accessible drag and drop
- Responsive column layout

**Primary Use Cases:** Project management tools, task tracking dashboards, agile workflow boards, content management pipelines, and any application requiring visual task organization.

**Compared to Alternatives:** This is a higher-level component built on react-beautiful-dnd rather than a standalone library. ## Animation

- [Framer Motion](https://www.framer.com/motion) - Production-ready animation library for React with gesture support, layout animations, and shared layout animations. Powers interactive components with minimal code. ([Read more](/details/framer-motion.md)) `Animations` `Gestures` `Interactions`
- [GSAP (GreenSock)](https://greensock.com/gsap/) - Industry-standard professional-grade animation platform with 23.6k stars. Excels at complex sequences, timeline control, and scroll animations with modular design. ([Read more](/details/gsap-greensock.md)) `Animation` `Timeline` `Scroll`
- [Lottie React](https://www.npmjs.com/package/lottie-react) - Seamless integration of vector animations from Adobe After Effects. Renders high-quality, scalable animations ideal for enhancing app aesthetics. ([Read more](/details/lottie-react.md)) `Lottie` `After Effects` `Vector`
- [Motion](https://motion.dev) - JavaScript and React animation library (formerly Framer Motion) with 18M monthly downloads, providing 120fps animations through hybrid engine combining Web Animations API with JavaScript flexibility. ([Read more](/details/motion.md)) `Animations` `Framer Motion` `Performance`
- [React Flip Move](https://github.com/joshwcomeau/react-flip-move) - Effortless animation between DOM changes (such as list reordering) using the FLIP technique, providing smooth transitions for elements that change position in the layout. ([Read more](/details/react-flip-move.md)) `Flip Technique` `List Reorder` `Transitions`
- [React Scroll Parallax](https://react-scroll-parallax.damnthat.tv) - React hooks and components for creating parallax scroll effects on banners, images, and DOM elements. Optimized for smooth performance with SSR support. ([Read more](/details/react-scroll-parallax.md)) `Parallax` `Scroll` `Effects`
- [React Spring](https://www.react-spring.dev) - Spring physics-based animation library for React providing fluid, natural animations through a physics simulation engine. Used for creating interactive and performant motion effects in modern React applications. ([Read more](/details/react-spring.md)) `Animations` `Physics` `Performance`
- [React Type Animation](https://react-type-animation.netlify.app) - Customizable typewriter component for React with sequence-based animations. Supports multiple strings, delays, backspacing, and cursor customization for landing pages. ([Read more](/details/react-type-animation.md)) `Typewriter` `Text Animation` `Effects`
- [Data Driven Motion](https://github.com/tkh44/data-driven-motion) - A React animation library that allows developers to easily animate data-driven visualizations, turning dataset changes into smooth visual transitions. ([Read more](/details/data-driven-motion.md)) `Data Driven` `Transitions` `Visualization`
- [Lottie-web](https://airbnb.io/lottie) - Library for rendering After Effects animations natively in the browser. Originally created by Airbnb, it has 29.9k+ GitHub stars and enables designers to export complex animations as JSON files that developers can embed and control programmatically. ([Read more](/details/lottie-web.md)) `After Effects` `Svg Rendering` `Bodymovin`
- [Matrix Card](https://github.com/MehmetKaplan/matrix-card) - A simple component to generate Matrix rain style cards in React, creating the iconic cascading characters effect. ([Read more](/details/matrix-card.md)) `Matrix` `Visual Effect` `Rain Effect`
- [Mo.js](https://mojs.github.io) - Motion graphics toolbelt for the web that provides a modular toolkit for creating complex animations, shape tweens, and motion graphic effects. It has 18.3k+ GitHub stars and is ideal for creating rich visual animations. ([Read more](/details/mojs.md)) `Motion Graphics` `Shape Animations` `Modular`
- [Motion-Primitives](https://motion-primitives.com/) - An open-source UI kit to make beautiful, animated interfaces faster, built for React, Next.js, and Tailwind CSS with pre-built animated components. ([Read more](/details/motion-primitives.md)) `Animation` `Framer Motion` `Ui Kit`
- [Popmotion](https://popmotion.io) - Popmotion is a functional, reactive JavaScript animation library offering incredible flexibility and customization. As a lower-level animation tool, it provides developers with fine-grained control over animations including springs, physics, and keyframe animations. ([Read more](/details/popmotion.md)) `Open Source` `Functional` `Physics Based`
- [React Animatable](https://github.com/inokawa/react-animatable) - An animation library for React using the Web Animations API, providing a modern and performant approach to animating components with native browser capabilities. ([Read more](/details/react-animatable.md)) `Web Animations Api` `Browser Native` `Transitions`
- [React Animations](https://github.com/FormidableLabs/react-animations) - React Animations brings the popular animate.css effects to React applications. It provides a collection of pre-defined animations like bounce, fade, and slide as JavaScript objects, compatible with any inline styling solution for easy integration. ([Read more](/details/react-animations.md)) `Open Source` `animate.css` `Inline Styles`
- [React Anime](https://github.com/stelatech/react-anime) - A super easy animation library for React, offering a simple API for adding animations and motion effects to components with minimal configuration. ([Read more](/details/react-anime.md)) `Simple Api` `Motion` `Transitions`
- [React Awesome Reveal](https://react-awesome-reveal.morello.dev) - An animation library for React that reveals elements with smooth animations as they enter the viewport, built on Intersection Observer for performance. ([Read more](/details/react-awesome-reveal.md)) `Animations` `Reveal` `Scroll` `Intersection Observer`
- [React Bits](https://github.com/DavidHDev/react-bits) - React Bits is a large, free collection of animated React components designed to enhance web applications. ([Read more](/details/vivus.md)) `Svg Animations` `Path Drawing` `Lightweight`

## UI Component Library

- [Chakra UI](https://chakra-ui.com) - React component library emphasizing developer experience, accessibility, and modularity with composable components and style props for flexible interface building. ([Read more](/details/chakra-ui.md)) `Accessible` `Composable` `Style Props`
- [Grommet](https://v2.grommet.io) - Grommet is an enterprise-grade React component library developed by Hewlett Packard Enterprise, focused on accessibility, responsiveness, and theming for complex web applications. It provides over 40 production-ready UI components with built-in WCAG compliance and internationalization support. Key features include comprehensive accessibility out-of-the-box with ARIA attributes, a powerful theming system with light/dark mode support, responsive layout components, and built-in internationalization. Primary use cases include enterprise dashboards, internal admin panels, complex SaaS applications, and any project requiring strict accessibility standards. Compared to Material UI (which has a larger community but heavier bundle) and Ant Design (more opinionated), Grommet offers superior accessibility defaults, flexible theming, and is purpose-built for enterprise-scale applications with strict compliance requirements. ([Read more](/details/grommet.md)) `Enterprise` `A11y` `React`
- [HeroUI (NextUI)](https://www.heroui.com/) - Beautiful, fast, and modern React UI library with 50+ components. Built on React Aria for accessibility with customizable themes and variants for diverse design needs. ([Read more](/details/heroui-nextui.md)) `UI Library` `Accessible` `Themeable`
- [Mantine](https://mantine.dev) - Fully functional React UI library with 100+ customizable components, 50+ hooks, TypeScript support, and 25k GitHub stars, offering flexibility and modern design patterns. ([Read more](/details/mantine.md)) `Typescript` `Open Source` `Hooks`
- [Next UI](https://nextui.org) - A popular React component library providing tabs, accordions, pagination, and other UI elements with extensive documentation and community support. ([Read more](/details/next-ui.md)) `Next UI` `Open Source` `React`
- [PrimeReact](https://primereact.org) - Rich open-source React component library with 100+ components designed for the PrimeNG ecosystem, offering 156k weekly NPM downloads and enterprise-grade UI components. ([Read more](/details/primereact.md)) `Enterprise` `Comprehensive` `Open Source`
- [Radix UI](https://radix-ui.com) - Low-level primitives for building accessible design systems with unstyled, composable components like Dialog, Dropdown, and Tooltip that serve as the foundation for libraries like shadcn/ui. ([Read more](/details/radix-ui.md)) `Accessible` `Headless` `Primitives`
- [Semantic UI React](https://react.semantic-ui.com) - Library for building user interfaces with clean HTML and consistent components, offering extensive customization options. ([Read more](/details/semantic-ui-react.md)) `Semantic UI` `Open Source` `React`
- [DaisyUI](https://daisyui.com/) - A popular, free Tailwind CSS component library that extends Tailwind with component class names, offering pure CSS components with zero JavaScript. ([Read more](/details/daisyui.md)) `Tailwind` `Css Only` `Components`
- [Fluent UI](https://react.fluentui.dev) - A data-driven UI component library based on Microsoft's design system, offering charts, graphs, and visualizations for React applications. ([Read more](/details/fluent-ui.md)) `Fluent UI` `Open Source` `React`
- [Headless UI](https://headlessui.com) - Headless UI is a set of completely unstyled, fully accessible UI components developed by the Tailwind CSS team, offering 45+ building blocks designed to integrate seamlessly with Tailwind CSS or any other styling approach. Unlike traditional component libraries, it provides behavior and accessibility without any visual styling — developers have complete control over appearance. Key features include fully WAI-ARIA compliant component patterns (Dialog, Popover, Menu, Listbox, Radio Group, Switch, Tabs, Disclosure, Combobox, Transitions), automatic focus management and keyboard navigation, headless (unstyled) architecture for complete design freedom, official React and Vue implementations, built-in transition/animation support, and 4+ million weekly npm downloads indicating strong ecosystem adoption. Primary use cases include custom design systems requiring accessible foundations, applications using Tailwind CSS needing polished interactive components, and teams wanting full control over visual design without sacrificing accessibility. Compared to Radix UI (more components but React-only) or Ariakit (hook-based approach), Headless UI is the simplest path to accessible components when using Tailwind CSS, though it offers fewer components than Radix. ([Read more](/details/headless-ui.md)) `Headless` `Open Source` `Tailwind Css`
- [KendoReact](https://www.telerik.com/kendo-react-ui) - A professional suite of 100+ native React components including grids, charts, schedulers, and editors, built from the ground up for React with no jQuery dependencies. ([Read more](/details/kendoreact.md)) `Enterprise` `Data Grid` `Charts` `Native React`
- [Material Tailwind](https://www.material-tailwind.com) - An open-source React UI library built with Tailwind CSS and Material Design principles. It provides ready-to-use components that combine Material Design's aesthetic with Tailwind CSS's utility-first styling approach. ([Read more](/details/material-tailwind.md)) `Tailwind Css` `Material Design` `Open Source`
- [Mobiscroll](https://mobiscroll.com/react) - A comprehensive UI library for React with advanced calendar, scheduler, date picker, and form components optimized for both desktop and mobile experiences. ([Read more](/details/mobiscroll.md)) `Calendar` `Scheduler` `Date Picker` `Mobile Friendly`
- [React Spectrum](https://react-spectrum.adobe.com/) - Adobe's React implementation of the Spectrum design system. Provides accessible, adaptive, and internationalized React components that work seamlessly across desktop and mobile devices. Built with React Aria hooks for maximum flexibility and accessibility compliance. ([Read more](/details/react-spectrum.md)) `Ui` `Design System` `Accessibility` `Adobe` `Spectrum`
- [React Suite](https://rsuitejs.com) - A library designed for middle platform and back-end products, offering a friendly development experience with ready-to-use UI components. ([Read more](/details/react-suite.md)) `React` `Open Source` `Back End`
- [React-Admin](https://marmelab.com/react-admin/) - React-Admin is a powerful framework for building admin user interfaces quickly with React, providing a comprehensive set of tools for CRUD operations and data visualization. It integrates seamlessly with REST/GraphQL APIs and supports customization through extensive plugin options. ([Read more](/details/react-admin.md)) `Admin Interface` `CRUD` `Open Source`
- [Shards React](https://designrevision.com/downloads/shards-react) - Open-source library of reusable React components for building modern web interfaces, available on DesignRevision. ([Read more](/details/shards-react.md)) `Open Source` `React Components` `Design System`
- [Syncfusion React Components](https://www.syncfusion.com/react-components) - A comprehensive suite of 80+ enterprise-grade React UI components including data grids, charts, schedulers, editors, and more with extensive features and professional support. ## Component Library

- [Ark UI](https://ark-ui.com/) - Ark UI is a modern, headless component library providing 45+ accessible, unstyled UI primitives that work seamlessly across React, Solid, Vue, and Svelte frameworks. Built by the Zag.js team, it leverages a state-machine architecture (XState) under the hood for predictable component behavior with complete styling freedom and WAI-ARIA compliance. Key features include framework-agnostic architecture, keyboard navigation and focus management, composable API design, tree-shakeable exports, and server-side rendering compatibility. Primary use cases include building cross-framework design systems, custom-styled accessible applications, and enterprise UI libraries that need consistent behavior across different frontend stacks. Compared to Radix UI (React/Vue-only) or Headless UI (Tailwind ecosystem only), Ark UI offers broader framework support with React, Solid, Vue, and Svelte all from a single codebase. ([Read more](/details/ark-ui.md)) `Headless` `Accessible` `Framework Agnostic`
- [Awesome React Components](https://github.com/brillout/awesome-react-components) - Awesome React Components is a curated directory of high-quality React libraries, components, and tools organized across functional categories including UI components, state management, routing, testing, and forms. It serves as a comprehensive discovery resource for developers seeking best-in-class solutions for common React development challenges. Key features include over 4,600 entries organized by category, annotations with metadata like GitHub stars and license information, community-maintained quality through open pull requests, and regularly updated listings with new additions. Primary use cases include library discovery for new projects, evaluating alternatives across multiple categories, and finding React solutions for specific UI or functional needs. Compared to npm search or unprioritized registries, this list provides human-curated quality assurance with community-vetted selections. ([Read more](/details/awesome-react-components.md)) `Open Source` `Curated List` `React Ecosystem`
- [Material UI (MUI)](https://mui.com/) - React component library based on Google's Material Design principles. Offers a wide range of buttons, navigation elements, and data tables. ([Read more](/details/material-ui-mui.md)) `Open Source` `Material Design` `Enterprise`
- [MUI (Material-UI)](https://mui.com/) - MUI is a popular React component library implementing Google's Material Design. It provides a wide range of ready-to-use UI components for building consistent and accessible web applications. ([Read more](/details/mui-material-ui.md)) `Material Design` `Open Source` `React`
- [shadcn/ui](https://ui.shadcn.com) - Open-source React component library built on Radix UI and Tailwind CSS with a copy-paste approach, offering the fastest-growing 'library' in the React ecosystem with highly customizable components. ([Read more](/details/shadcnui.md)) `Copy Paste` `Tailwind Css` `Radix Ui`

- [Atlaskit](https://atlaskit.atlassian.com/packages) - Atlaskit is Atlassian's official React UI component library, providing a comprehensive design system with 100+ components for building enterprise applications that match Atlassian's design language and user experience standards. It covers everything from basic UI elements (badges, buttons, icons) to complex components (tree tables, date pickers, drag-and-drop boards) and design tokens for consistent theming. Key features include enterprise-grade accessibility, comprehensive documentation with live examples, TypeScript support, Storybook integration for component exploration, and alignment with the Atlassian Design System. Primary use cases include building Jira/Confluence-like enterprise applications, internal tools, and SaaS products requiring a polished, corporate-grade UI. Compared to open-source alternatives like Material UI or Ant Design, Atlaskit offers a more refined enterprise aesthetic with Atlassian's battle-tested patterns, though it has a narrower scope focused on Atlassian's specific design philosophy. ([Read more](/details/atlaskit.md)) `Enterprise` `Atlassian` `Comprehensive`
- [Base Web](https://baseweb.design) - Base Web (also known as Base UI) is a React component library developed by Uber that serves as a foundation for building enterprise web applications. It provides a comprehensive set of well-engineered, themeable components with built-in accessibility and internationalization support. Key features include an extensible component architecture for deep customization, a powerful theme system with design tokens for light/dark modes, a comprehensive grid and layout system, and support for RTL languages with full accessibility. Primary use cases include enterprise dashboards, internal tools, data-heavy applications, and design system foundations. Compared to MUI (which is more feature-rich but heavier) or Ant Design (more opinionated), Base Web offers a unique overrides system that enables deep component customization while maintaining consistent design language, making it ideal for teams needing fine-grained control over component behavior. ## Rich Text Editors

- [MDXEditor](https://mdxeditor.dev/) - Open-source WYSIWYG editor for MDX content built on the Lexical framework. Provides inline editing where formatting appears as you type, with no separate preview pane needed. ([Read more](/details/mdxeditor.md)) `Markdown` `Wysiwyg` `Mdx`
- [Quill](https://quilljs.com) - Free, open-source rich text editor with granular API access to content, changes, and events, using JSON as both input and output for powerful text editing capabilities. ([Read more](/details/quill.md)) `Rich Text Editor` `Wysiwyg` `Text Editing`
- [react-syntax-highlighter](https://github.com/react-syntax-highlighter/react-syntax-highlighter) - Syntax highlighting component for React supporting Prism or Highlight libraries, using syntax trees to efficiently update only changing DOM elements with inline styles. ([Read more](/details/react-syntax-highlighter.md)) `Syntax Highlighting` `Code Display` `Prism`
- [Slate](https://docs.slatejs.org) - Framework for building customizable rich text editors within React applications with plugin architecture, providing flexibility and extensibility for diverse text editing needs. ([Read more](/details/slate.md)) `Rich Text Editor` `Framework` `Extensible`
- [Tiptap](https://www.tiptap.dev) - Headless rich-text editor framework built on ProseMirror, designed for developers to create highly customizable editors through a modular, extension-based architecture. ([Read more](/details/tiptap.md)) `Rich Text Editor` `Headless` `Extensions`
- [BlockNote](https://www.blocknotejs.org) - BlockNote is a modern, block-based rich text editor for React built on top of ProseMirror and TipTap, providing a Notion-like editing experience with drag-and-drop blocks, slash commands, and AI integration capabilities. It features a clean, intuitive interface for content creation with real-time collaboration support through Yjs CRDT protocol. Key features include drag-and-drop block reordering, slash command menus for formatting, real-time collaborative editing, customizable block types, AI-assisted content generation, full TypeScript support, WAI-ARIA accessibility compliance, light and dark theme support, markdown shortcuts, and export to HTML/Markdown. Primary use cases include document editors, knowledge base platforms, content management systems, collaborative writing tools, and any application requiring a rich text editor with block-based composition. Compared to Quill or CKEditor (which are inline-formatting focused), BlockNote offers a more modern block-based editing paradigm similar to Notion, while compared to Tiptap (which is lower-level), BlockNote provides a more opinionated, ready-to-use experience. ([Read more](/details/blocknote.md)) `Rich Text Editor` `Wysiwyg` `Block Editor` `Collaboration`
- [CKEditor 5 for React](https://ckeditor.com/ckeditor-5/react/) - The official React integration for CKEditor 5, a powerful WYSIWYG HTML editor with modern features including real-time collaboration, markdown support, and extensive customization options. - [Froala Editor React](https://froala.com/wysiwyg-editor/docs/framework-plugins/react/) - A beautiful, lightweight WYSIWYG HTML editor optimized for performance with powerful features including inline editing, image management, and extensive plugin support. ([Read more](/details/froala-editor-react.md)) `Wysiwyg` `Rich Text Editor` `Inline Editing` `Lightweight`
- [Jodit React](https://xdsoft.net/jodit/) - A lightweight, open-source WYSIWYG editor for React with no dependencies, offering a fast alternative to TinyMCE and CKEditor with modern features and customization. ([Read more](/details/jodit-react.md)) `Wysiwyg` `Rich Text Editor` `Lightweight` `Open Source`
- [Lexical](https://lexical.dev) - An extensible text editor framework built by Meta (Facebook) for React, designed to provide reliable, accessible, and performant text editing experiences with complete customization. ([Read more](/details/lexical.md)) `Rich Text Editor` `Framework` `Facebook` `Extensible`
- [ProseMirror](https://prosemirror.net) - A toolkit for building rich-text editors with a document model that enables real-time collaborative editing, used as the foundation for many popular editors like TipTap and Atlassian's editor. ([Read more](/details/prosemirror.md)) `Rich Text Editor` `Toolkit` `Collaboration` `Low Level`
- [React Contenteditable](https://github.com/lovasoa/react-contenteditable) - Contenteditable wrapper component for React enabling inline text editing. Provides controlled component interface for editable content. ([Read more](/details/react-contenteditable.md)) `Editable` `Contenteditable` `Inline Editing`

Integrates with Highlight.js for comprehensive language support. ([Read more](/details/react-highlight.md)) `Syntax Highlighting` `Code` `Themes`

Useful for search results, text matching, and content highlighting with customizable styling. ([Read more](/details/react-highlight-words.md)) `Highlight` `Text Matching` `Search`

Provides flexible markdown parsing and rendering for displaying formatted text content. ([Read more](/details/react-markdown.md)) `Markdown` `Rendering` `Open Source`

Lightweight at ~4.6 kB gzipped with syntax highlighting support. ([Read more](/details/react-markdown-editor.md)) `Markdown` `Editor` `Lightweight`
- [React Rich Text Editor](https://github.com/LukasMasuch/react-rich-text) - React Rich Text Editor is a feature-rich WYSIWYG editing component for React applications that provides a modern collaborative writing experience with markdown support, real-time preview, and drag-and-drop file insertion. It enables users to compose formatted content with a familiar toolbar interface while maintaining a clean, customizable design. Key features include drag-and-drop file insertion for images and documents, real-time collaborative editing with multiple user cursors, markdown and HTML export options, customizable toolbar with modular plugin architecture, offline storage support for uninterrupted editing, and accessible keyboard shortcuts conforming to WCAG guidelines. Primary use cases include blog authoring platforms, CMS content editing interfaces, comment and review systems, email composition tools, document collaboration apps, and any React application requiring rich content creation. Compared to Quill (which requires manual React integration) or Slate.js (more powerful but requires significantly more setup), this editor provides a ready-to-use experience with collaboration features out of the box. ## Charts & Visualizations

- [Nivo](https://nivo.rocks) - Rich data visualization library offering wide selection of chart components driven by D3.js, with built-in motion, theming, and server-side rendering support. ([Read more](/details/nivo.md)) `Charts` `d3.js` `Data Visualization`
- [React ApexCharts](https://apexcharts.com/docs/react-charts) - Modern charting library wrapper for React with 30+ chart types, real-time updates, and interactive candlestick charts. Perfect for financial dashboards and live data visualization. ([Read more](/details/react-apexcharts.md)) `Charts` `Visualization` `Real Time`
- [Recharts](https://recharts.org) - Composable chart library built on React components for easy data visualization, renowned for flexibility and becoming the most popular way to deliver visualizations in the React ecosystem. ([Read more](/details/recharts.md)) `Charts` `Data Visualization` `Composable`
- [Tremor](https://www.tremor.so/) - Open-source React UI components styled with Tailwind CSS specifically designed for building charts and dashboards. Features 35+ fully accessible components built with React, Tailwind CSS, and Radix UI. ([Read more](/details/tremor.md)) `Open Source` `Tailwind Css` `Dashboard`
- [Highcharts React](https://github.com/highcharts/highcharts-react) - Official React wrapper for Highcharts, the industry-leading charting library. Provides comprehensive charting capabilities with extensive customization options, interactive features, and professional-grade visualizations. Supports all Highcharts modules and extensions. ([Read more](/details/highcharts-react.md)) `Charts` `Highcharts` `Enterprise` `Visualization`
- [React Chart.js 2](https://react-chartjs-2.js.org) - React components for Chart.js, providing a simple way to create responsive, animated charts with excellent performance using canvas rendering for large datasets. ([Read more](/details/react-chartjs-2.md)) `Charts` `Data Visualization` `Canvas` `Performance`
- [React ChartJS](https://github.com/reactchartjs/react-chartjs-2) - React components for Chart.js, the popular HTML5 charting library. Provides easy-to-use React wrappers for all Chart.js chart types with TypeScript support. Includes hooks for direct chart instance access and custom plugin integration. ([Read more](/details/react-chartjs.md)) `Charts` `Chartjs` `Graphs` `Visualization`
- [Victory](https://victory.js.org) - React charting library from Formidable focusing on modular building blocks with consistent API, accessibility helpers, and ARIA labels that come standard with interactive charts. ([Read more](/details/victory.md)) `Charts` `Modular` `Accessible`
- [Visx](https://visx-viz.github.io) - Low-level D3.js primitives from Airbnb wrapped in React, providing small, tree-shakable components with full control over styling and layout for high-performance visualizations. ([Read more](/details/visx.md)) `d3.js` `Primitives` `Performance`

## Data Visualization

- [Apache ECharts](https://echarts.apache.org/) - Apache ECharts is a powerful, interactive data visualization library maintained by the Apache Software Foundation, excelling at rendering complex charts from small datasets to massive real-time streams with tens of thousands of data points. It uses canvas and WebGL rendering for optimal performance and provides a comprehensive charting API with 20+ chart types including line, bar, scatter, pie, radar, candlestick, heatmap, treemap, sankey, and graph visualizations. Key features include WebGL-accelerated rendering for large datasets, real-time data streaming, rich interaction controls (zoom, pan, brush selection), multiple coordinate systems (Cartesian, polar, geo), and built-in animation framework. Primary use cases include business intelligence dashboards, financial charting platforms, real-time monitoring systems, IoT data displays, and analytics applications. Compared to D3.js (more flexible but lower-level) or Chart.js (simpler but less capable), ECharts offers a powerful middle ground with high-level APIs, exceptional rendering performance, and extensive visualization types. ([Read more](/details/apache-echarts.md)) `Charts` `Big Data` `Webgl`
- [React Map GL](https://github.com/visgl/react-map-gl) - React wrapper for Mapbox GL, providing interactive maps with layers, markers, and complex visualizations. Enables building map-based interfaces with full customization and real-time updates. ([Read more](/details/react-map-gl.md)) `Maps` `Geospatial` `Mapbox`
- [SVAR React Gantt](https://svar.dev/react/gantt) - Open-source high-performance Gantt chart with interactive timeline, drag-and-drop task management, dependencies, and TypeScript support. MIT licensed for commercial use. ([Read more](/details/svar-react-gantt.md)) `Gantt Chart` `Timeline` `Project Management`
- [three.js](https://threejs.org) - JavaScript 3D library that renders WebGL-powered graphics. The most popular JavaScript 3D rendering engine, providing 3D visualization capabilities for React applications through React Three Fiber. ([Read more](/details/threejs.md)) `3D` `Webgl` `Open Source`
- [Ant Design Charts](https://ant-design-charts.antgroup.com/en) - Ant Design Charts is a React charting library built on G2Plot, offering a comprehensive suite of statistical and business visualization components that seamlessly integrate with the Ant Design ecosystem. It provides 20+ chart types including line, bar, pie, area, scatter, radar, funnel, gauge, and waterfall charts, all rendered on Canvas for optimal performance with large datasets. Key features include intelligent auto-layout and responsive design, built-in tooltips and legends, robust theming with Ant Design design tokens, and accessibility-focused configurations. Primary use cases include business intelligence dashboards, analytics platforms, financial reporting tools, and any React application requiring rich data visualization within the Ant Design UI system. Compared to Recharts (which uses SVG and has simpler APIs) or Apache ECharts (more powerful but steeper learning curve), Ant Design Charts offers the best balance of developer experience and visual quality for React projects already using Ant Design, though it's less customizable than lower-level libraries like D3.js. ([Read more](/details/ant-design-charts.md)) `Canvas` `React Components` `Ui Framework`
- [AnyChart](https://www.anychart.com) - Interactive JavaScript charting library supporting React, Angular, Vue, and vanilla JS. Provides TypeScript definitions and flexible customization for building rich data visualizations across multiple frameworks. ([Read more](/details/anychart.md)) `Javascript` `Charts` `Multi Framework`
- [ApexCharts](https://apexcharts.com) - ApexCharts is a modern, interactive open-source charting library for JavaScript that provides rich, customizable data visualizations with a simple API. It supports 14+ chart types including line, area, bar, column, pie, donut, scatter, bubble, heatmap, and candlestick charts, with interactive tooltips, zooming, panning, and real-time data updates. Key features include responsive design with automatic resizing, dynamic chart updates, export to PNG/SVG/CSV, and official wrappers for React, Angular, Vue, and Svelte. Primary use cases include business dashboards, analytics platforms, financial applications, and any project requiring beautiful interactive charts. Compared to Chart.js (simpler but less feature-rich) and D3.js (more flexible but more complex), ApexCharts offers an excellent balance of ease-of-use and visual quality with built-in interactivity. ([Read more](/details/apexcharts.md)) `Open Source` `Charts` `Multi Framework`
- [billboard.js](https://naver.github.io/billboard.js/) - billboard.js is a reusable, easy-to-use JavaScript chart library developed by Naver, built on top of D3.js v5+ (later versions use D3 v6+). It provides a simplified declarative API for creating interactive data visualizations with minimal configuration while leveraging D3's powerful rendering engine under the hood. Key features include support for line, bar, pie, donut, gauge, area, scatter, radar, heatmap, treemap, bubble, and spline charts, built-in interactivity with tooltips and zooming, responsive design with automatic resizing, multiple built-in themes including d3-dark, and official React wrapper (@billboard.js/react). Primary use cases include business dashboards, analytics platforms, statistical data displays, and web applications requiring fast implementation of beautiful charts. Compared to Chart.js (simpler but less customizable) or D3.js directly (more powerful but requires significantly more code), billboard.js strikes a balance by offering the rendering quality and flexibility of D3 with a much friendlier, configuration-driven API. ([Read more](/details/billboardjs.md)) `Charts` `D3` `Visualization`
- [BizCharts](https://github.com/alibaba/BizCharts) - BizCharts is a React charting library developed by Alibaba's AntV team, built on top of G2 (a visualization grammar engine based on D3). It provides declarative chart components for building business data visualizations with an intuitive JSX syntax. Key features include support for line, bar, pie, scatter, area, funnel, radar, and heat map charts, declarative grammar-based chart composition, configurable axes and legends, and responsive resizing. Primary use cases include business intelligence dashboards, analytics applications, reporting tools, and any React project needing customizable chart visualizations. Note that BizCharts v3 and earlier are based on AntV G2; Ant Design Charts is the newer charting library from the same team that supersedes BizCharts for new projects. Compared to Recharts (simpler grammar, larger community in Western markets), BizCharts offers more sophisticated visualization grammar but with a steeper learning curve. ([Read more](/details/bizcharts.md)) `Alibaba` `G2` `Business Charts`
- [Chart.js](https://www.chartjs.org/) - Simple yet flexible JavaScript charting library for designers and developers, providing a set of frequently used chart types, plugins, and customization options. It is the most popular charting library by GitHub stars and npm downloads. ([Read more](/details/chartjs.md)) `Charts` `Open Source` `Responsive`

Primary use cases include analytics dashboards, financial reporting applications, business intelligence platforms, KPI tracking interfaces, and any React project needing interactive chart visualizations. It supports multiple color models — RGB, HSL, HEX, HSV, and HSLuv — along with real-time preview, color history, and a small footprint under 5KB gzipped with zero dependencies. Key features include 8+ pre-built color picker styles matching popular design systems, support for RGB/HSL/HEX/HSV color models with real-time preview, color swatches and history tracking for quick reuse, theme customization to match any design system, TypeScript definitions for type safety, and a zero-dependency architecture keeping bundle size minimal. Primary use cases include theme customization panels, brand color selection tools, designer handoff interfaces, and any React application requiring user-controlled color input. Compared to react-color (a different package with ~30 external dependencies and 300+ KB bundle), this library achieves similar functionality with zero dependencies and a fraction of the size, making it ideal for performance-conscious projects. - [React Form Builder](https://github.com/transformap/react-form-builder) - Drag-and-drop form builder component that allows users to create dynamic forms at runtime with validation and export capabilities. ([Read more](/details/react-form-builder.md)) `Open Source` `Form Builder` `Dynamic Forms`
- [React Form Validation](https://github.com/airjp73/react-validation) - React Form Validation is a lightweight, schema-based form validation library for React that provides declarative validation rules with real-time feedback, custom error messaging, and integration with any form structure. It supports both synchronous field-level validation and asynchronous server-side checks for complex scenarios like username availability. Key features include declarative schema-based validation configuration using simple JavaScript objects, real-time validation on input change, blur, and submit events, custom error message definitions with dynamic placeholders for field names and requirements, async validation support for server-side checks like email uniqueness or code availability, conditional validation rules that activate based on other field values or form state, and zero external dependencies keeping bundle size minimal. Primary use cases include user registration and login forms with complex password requirements, checkout forms with address and payment validation, multi-step wizards with per-step validation, and admin data entry interfaces requiring strict data integrity. Compared to larger form libraries like Formik with Yup (which add significant bundle weight) or React Hook Form's native Zod integration (which requires external schema libraries), this library provides validation capabilities with zero dependencies, though it lacks the broader form state management features of full form libraries. ([Read more](/details/react-form-validation.md)) `Form Validation` `Open Source` `Zero Dependencies`
- [React Form Validator](https://github.com/brillout/react-form-validator) - React Form Validator is a schema-based form validation library for React that provides real-time validation feedback with customizable rules, error messages, and async validation support for server-side checks. It integrates seamlessly with any React form architecture and supports nested object schemas for complex form structures. Key features include declarative schema-based validation configuration with a fluent API, real-time inline error display on field blur and input change, async validation for checking username availability or email uniqueness, custom validation rule definitions with TypeScript support, conditional validation rules that depend on other field values, and seamless integration with React Hook Form, Formik, and standalone forms. Primary use cases include registration and login forms, multi-step checkout flows, admin panel data entry, and any application requiring robust client-side validation before form submission. Compared to Yup (schema-only, requires additional form integration) or react-hook-form's built-in validation (tied to that specific form library), this validator is framework-agnostic and provides richer real-time UX with built-in error message management.
