## Tables & Datagrids

- [AG Grid React](https://www.ag-grid.com/react-data-grid/) - AG Grid React provides the industry-leading JavaScript data grid with full React integration, offering both a free community edition and a feature-rich enterprise version. It delivers spreadsheet-like performance with advanced data operations including row grouping, pivoting, aggregation, and virtual scrolling. The React wrapper enables seamless component rendering within cells and supports modern React patterns.

• Free community edition with sorting, filtering, pagination, and cell editing
• Enterprise features: row grouping, aggregation, pivot tables, and Excel export
• Virtual scrolling handles millions of rows efficiently
• Full React component integration for custom cell renderers and editors

Primary use cases include financial dashboards, data analysis tools, ERP systems, admin panels, and any application requiring complex tabular data presentation. Compared to alternatives like react-table (headless, requires more setup) or Handsontable (spreadsheet-focused), AG Grid offers the most comprehensive feature set with both free and commercial licensing options. ([Read more](/details/ag-grid-react.md)) `Data Grid` `Enterprise` `Performance`
- [React Datasheet Grid](https://react-datasheet-grid.netlify.app) - Excel-like data grid optimized for speed with virtualized architecture. Handles hundreds of thousands of rows with copy/paste support from Excel and Google Sheets. ([Read more](/details/react-datasheet-grid.md)) `Spreadsheet` `Data Grid` `Excel`
- [React Window](https://react-window.vercel.app) - Efficient React component for rendering large lists and grids. Uses virtualization to render only visible items, enabling smooth scrolling through millions of items with minimal performance impact. ([Read more](/details/react-window.md)) `Virtualization` `Performance` `Lists`
- [TanStack Table](https://tanstack.com/table/latest) - Headless UI for building powerful tables and datagrids across React, Vue, Solid, and Svelte, featuring sorting, filtering, pagination, row selection, and 10-15kb lightweight bundle. ([Read more](/details/tanstack-table.md)) `Table` `Datagrid` `Headless`
- [Glide Data Grid](https://grid.glideapps.com) - A lightning-fast, no-compromise data grid for React with rich rendering capabilities, handling millions of rows with smooth 60fps scrolling and full TypeScript support. ([Read more](/details/glide-data-grid.md)) `Data Grid` `Performance` `Virtualization` `Typescript`
- [Handsontable React](https://handsontable.com/docs/react-data-grid/) - A JavaScript spreadsheet component for React that mimics Excel behavior, offering familiar spreadsheet features like formulas, data validation, and cell formatting for data-intensive applications. ([Read more](/details/handsontable-react.md)) `Spreadsheet` `Data Grid` `Excel Like` `Formulas`
- [React Infinite Scroll](https://github.com/tobiasbueschel/react-infinite-scroll-component) - Infinite scroll component for React with support for virtual scrolling and lazy loading. Automatically loads more content as user scrolls to bottom. ([Read more](/details/react-infinite-scroll.md)) `Infinite Scroll` `Lazy Loading` `Performance`
- [React JSON Table](https://github.com/azendev/react-json-table) - React JSON Table is a zero-configuration table component that automatically renders JavaScript objects and JSON arrays into interactive, sortable, and filterable data tables with built-in pagination support. It analyzes data structure on-the-fly to generate columns and supports deeply nested object paths for complex data shapes. Key features include automatic column generation from JSON keys, multi-column sorting with ascending/descending toggle, real-time filtering across all columns with case-insensitive matching, built-in pagination with configurable page sizes, custom cell renderers using React components for rich data display, row selection with single or multi-select modes, and responsive design that adapts table layout to available viewport width. Primary use cases include API response data exploration, developer tools and admin panels displaying JSON data, data import preview screens, debugging interfaces for examining object structures, and quick data grids for prototype applications. Compared to heavier table libraries like ag-Grid or MUI DataGrid (which require extensive configuration for basic use), React JSON Table provides instant table rendering from raw JSON with zero schema definition, though it lacks advanced features like inline editing, virtualization for very large datasets, or column pinning. ([Read more](/details/react-json-table.md)) `Open Source` `JSON` `Data Table`
- [React Spreadsheet Grid](https://denisraslov.github.io/grid) - Excel-like grid component with custom cell editors, performant scroll, and resizable columns. Supports keyboard control, lazy loading, and TypeScript. ([Read more](/details/react-spreadsheet-grid.md)) `Spreadsheet` `Excel` `Data Grid`
- [React Table Component](https://github.com/tannerlinsley/react-table) - A highly customizable table component with features like sorting, pagination, and filtering for React applications. ([Read more](/details/react-table-component.md)) `Open Source` `Data Table` `React Table`
- [React Table Library](https://github.com/BasixKOR/react-table-library) - Headless table library for building powerful, accessible data tables. Provides table logic without forcing specific UI or styling, allowing complete customization. ([Read more](/details/react-table-library.md)) `Table` `Datagrid` `Headless`
- [React Virtualized Table](https://github.com/bvaughn/react-virtualized) - React Virtualized Table is a high-performance data table component built on top of react-virtualized's windowing engine, designed to render large datasets with thousands of rows while maintaining smooth 60fps scrolling and minimal memory consumption. It only renders the rows and columns currently visible in the viewport, dramatically reducing DOM node count and improving responsiveness. Key features include row and column virtualization for efficient large dataset rendering, auto-measuring row heights for variable content, fixed or dynamic column widths with resizing support, column sorting with customizable sort functions, sticky headers and column headers that remain visible during scroll, keyboard navigation support for accessibility compliance, and custom cell renderers with React component injection. Primary use cases include enterprise data grids displaying hundreds of thousands of records, admin panels with sortable and filterable data tables, log viewers and audit trails with extensive row counts, and financial applications with real-time data streaming tables. Compared to building tables with plain HTML (which crashes with large datasets) or modern alternatives like ag-Grid React (commercial, more features but heavier), React Virtualized Table provides a proven, open-source windowing solution optimized specifically for React at a fraction of the bundle cost. ([Read more](/details/react-virtualized-table.md)) `Open Source` `Virtualization` `Performance`
- [react-data-grid](https://github.com/Comcast/react-data-grid) - Feature-rich and customizable data grid React component from Comcast with support for custom cell renderers, inline editing, and sophisticated data management capabilities. ([Read more](/details/react-data-grid.md)) `Datagrid` `Data Table` `Customizable`
- [react-paginate](https://github.com/AdeleD/react-paginate) - Popular pagination component library for React with easy installation and good customization options, used by 657+ projects with flexible implementation. ([Read more](/details/react-paginate.md)) `Pagination` `Navigation` `Customizable`
- [SVAR React DataGrid](https://svar.dev/react/datagrid/) - A lightweight, open-source React data grid with enterprise features including virtual scrolling, inline editing, sorting, filtering, and TypeScript support, designed for modern applications. ([Read more](/details/svar-react-datagrid.md)) `Data Grid` `Virtualization` `Open Source` `Typescript`

## Data Fetching

- [Apollo Client](https://github.com/apollographql/apollo-client) - Apollo Client is a comprehensive state management and GraphQL data-fetching library for JavaScript applications. It provides a complete solution for interacting with GraphQL servers, featuring normalized caching, optimistic UI updates, real-time subscriptions, and built-in pagination helpers. Key features include automatic cache normalization, declarative data fetching via hooks, error handling, and seamless integration with React through @apollo/react-hooks. Primary use cases include building complex data-driven SPAs, dashboards requiring real-time updates, and applications with sophisticated caching needs. Compared to alternatives like urql (which is smaller and focuses on simplicity) or raw fetch with SWR/React Query, Apollo Client offers the most feature-complete GraphQL experience with a powerful normalized cache and DevTools, though it comes with a larger bundle size. ([Read more](/details/apollo-client.md)) `Graphql` `Caching` `Subscriptions`
- [React Relay](https://github.com/facebook/relay) - A JavaScript framework for building data-driven React applications developed by Meta. Provides a declarative approach to data fetching with colocation and automatic batching. ([Read more](/details/react-relay.md)) `Graphql` `Fragment Colocation` `Facebook`
- [TanStack Query](https://github.com/TanStack/query) - Powerful asynchronous state management, server-state utilities and data fetching for TS/JS, React, Solid, Svelte and Vue. Provides caching, synchronization, and state management for server state. ([Read more](/details/tanstack-query.md)) `Server State` `Caching` `Multi Framework`
- [Axios React](https://github.com/soroushchehresa/axios-react) - Axios React provides a declarative, component-based wrapper around the popular Axios HTTP client library, enabling HTTP requests to be expressed as React components rather than imperative function calls. It simplifies data fetching patterns by allowing developers to declaratively specify requests using JSX syntax with automatic lifecycle management.

**Key Features:**
- Declarative HTTP requests as React components
- Automatic request execution and cleanup on unmount
- Loading, error, and data state management built-in
- Built on top of Axios with full interceptor support
- TypeScript definitions included
- Request deduplication and cancellation support

**Primary Use Cases:** Ideal for React applications preferring declarative data fetching patterns, component-level HTTP configuration, and teams already using Axios who want a more React-idiomatic interface.

**Compared to Alternatives:** Unlike React Query or SWR (which focus on caching and server state management), axios-react is a thin declarative wrapper with no caching layer. It's simpler but less feature-rich than hooks-based data fetching libraries like use-axios-client. ([Read more](/details/axios-react.md)) `Http Client` `Declarative` `Axios`
- [React Refetch](https://github.com/heroku/react-refetch) - A simple, declarative, and composable way to fetch data for React components. Uses higher-order components to connect data fetching to component props. ([Read more](/details/react-refetch.md)) `Declarative` `Higher Order Component` `Data Fetching`
- [Redux Connect](https://github.com/makeomatic/redux-connect) - Provides decorator for resolving async props in React Router. Enables data fetching through Redux before rendering routed components. ([Read more](/details/redux-connect.md)) `Async Props` `React Router` `Server Rendering`
- [Resourcerer](https://github.com/SiftScience/resourcerer) - Declarative data-fetching framework for REST APIs. Provides a React-based approach to fetching, caching, and managing API data with minimal boilerplate. ([Read more](/details/resourcerer.md)) `REST` `Declarative` `Caching`

## State Management

- [React Router](https://reactrouter.com/en/main) - The most popular routing library for React, handling client-side navigation and linking components together for single-page applications. ([Read more](/details/react-router.md)) `Routing` `Open Source` `React`
- [Redux](https://redux.js.org) - A predictable state container for JavaScript apps, widely used for managing application state in React applications. ([Read more](/details/redux.md)) `state management` `Open Source` `React`
- [SWR](https://swr.vercel.app) - React hooks library for data fetching with support for caching, revalidation, and focus tracking. Implements stale-while-revalidate pattern for performant data fetching. ([Read more](/details/swr.md)) `Data Fetching` `Hooks` `Caching`
- [Baobab React](https://github.com/Yomguithereal/baobab-react) - Baobab React provides React integration for Baobab, a persistent and immutable data structure library that manages state in a tree-like format with cursor-based access patterns. It enables components to subscribe to specific branches of a state tree and automatically re-render when relevant data changes. Key features include immutable persistent data structures, cursor-based state access with granular subscriptions, automatic re-rendering on targeted state changes, and built-in time-travel debugging support. Primary use cases include complex state management in applications where immutability and traceability are important, state trees requiring hierarchical organization, and situations where time-travel debugging provides value. Compared to Redux (which uses a flat state tree and actions) or Immer (mutable API with immutable results), Baobab offers a unique cursor-based approach with built-in persistence and history tracking. ([Read more](/details/baobab-react.md)) `Immutable` `Data Structure` `Tree State`
- [Cerebral](https://github.com/cerebral/cerebral) - A state controller with its own debugger for React applications. Provides a predictable, centralized approach to managing application state with built-in debugging tools. ([Read more](/details/cerebral.md)) `State Management` `Debugger` `Centralized`
- [Effector React](https://github.com/effector/effector) - React bindings for Effector, an effective multi-store state manager for JavaScript applications. Provides reactive primitives and hooks for managing complex application state. ([Read more](/details/effector-react.md)) `State Management` `Multi Store` `React Bindings`
- [Fluxible](https://github.com/yahoo/fluxible) - A pluggable container for universal flux applications from Yahoo. Provides a structured approach to data flow with support for server-side rendering and client hydration. ([Read more](/details/fluxible.md)) `Flux` `Universal` `Isomorphic`
- [Immer](https://immerjs.github.io/immer/) - A library that simplifies immutable state updates by letting you write code that looks like it mutates state, while maintaining immutability through JavaScript Proxies. ([Read more](/details/immer.md)) `Immutable` `State` `Redux`
- [Jotai](https://jotai.org/) - Primitive and flexible state management for React with an atomic model, offering ~2M weekly downloads and bottom-up approach to global state. ([Read more](/details/jotai.md)) `Atoms` `State` `Minimal`
- [Kea](https://github.com/mariusandra/kea) - High level architecture for React apps that provides a structured way to manage logic, state, and side effects. Uses a declarative syntax to define reusable logic modules. ([Read more](/details/kea.md)) `Redux` `Logic` `Architecture`
- [MobX](https://mobx.js.org) - MobX is a state management library for React that uses observable data structures to automatically track state changes and update components. It simplifies state management with reactive data binding and minimal boilerplate code. ([Read more](/details/mobx.md)) `Reactive State` `Observables` `Open Source`
- [Nano Stores](https://github.com/nanostores/nanostores) - Ultra-lightweight state management library for JavaScript applications. Provides a minimal, fast, and framework-agnostic approach to managing global state with support for React through a dedicated integration package. ([Read more](/details/nano-stores.md)) `Lightweight` `Framework Agnostic` `Reactive`
- [NextAuth.js](https://next-auth.js.org) - NextAuth.js is a developer-friendly authentication library for React applications built with Next.js. It supports OAuth, email, and database authentication providers with built-in session management and user profile handling. ([Read more](/details/nextauthjs.md)) `SSO` `OAuth` `Next.js`
- [React i18next](https://react.i18next.com) - Internationalization framework for React with full support for multiple languages, namespaces, and translations. Provides hooks and HOCs for integrating i18n into React components. ([Read more](/details/react-i18next.md)) `I18n` `Internationalization` `Localization`
- [React Query](https://tanstack.com/query/v4) - React Query is a data fetching and state management library that simplifies retrieving, caching, and updating server state in React applications. It provides declarative data handling with built-in support for pagination, sorting, and query invalidation. ([Read more](/details/react-query.md)) `Data Fetching` `State Management` `Open Source`
- [React Query DevTools](https://github.com/tanstack/query) - Developer tools for React Query providing real-time visibility into queries, cache state, and debugging. Essential companion for building and debugging React Query applications. ([Read more](/details/react-query-devtools.md)) `Debugging` `Devtools` `React Query`
- [React Redux](https://react-redux.js.org/) - Official React bindings for Redux. Provides React hooks (useSelector, useDispatch) and components for integrating Redux state management with React applications. Optimized for performance with automatic render optimization and selector memoization. ([Read more](/details/react-redux.md)) `Redux` `State` `Hooks` `Global State`
- [React Router DOM](https://reactrouter.com) - DOM bindings for React Router providing components and hooks for building single-page applications with client-side routing. Standard routing solution for React web applications. ([Read more](/details/react-router-dom.md)) `Routing` `Dom Bindings` `Spa`
- [Recoil](https://recoiljs.org) - Recoil is a state management library for React developed by Facebook, offering a simple API for managing global state with atom-based data containers. It emphasizes simplicity and performance for medium to large applications.
 ([Read more](/details/recoil.md)) `Facebook` `Atom Based` `Reactive State`
- [Redux Auth](https://github.com/lynndylanhurley/redux-auth) - Complete token authentication system for React and Redux that supports isomorphic rendering. Provides authentication flow with Redux store integration. ([Read more](/details/redux-auth.md)) `Authentication` `Isomorphic` `Tokens`
- [Redux Batched Actions](https://github.com/tshelburne/redux-batched-actions) - Redux utility that combines multiple actions into a single dispatch, triggering only one subscriber notification. Improves performance by reducing re-renders. ([Read more](/details/redux-batched-actions.md)) `Redux` `Performance` `Batching`
- [Redux First History](https://github.com/salvoravida/redux-first-history) - Redux history binding supporting React Router, Reach Router, and Wouter. Keeps Redux and router history in sync for unified state management. ([Read more](/details/redux-first-history.md)) `Router` `History Binding` `Redux`
- [Redux Saga](https://redux-saga.js.org/) - A middleware library for handling side effects in Redux applications using ES6 Generators. Makes async flows easy to read, test, and handle. Provides powerful patterns for managing complex async workflows, API calls, and background tasks. ([Read more](/details/redux-saga.md)) `Redux` `Middleware` `Async` `Side Effects`
- [Redux Search](https://github.com/treasure-data/redux-search) - Redux bindings for client-side search. Provides Redux integration for connecting search results to your Redux store. ([Read more](/details/redux-search.md)) `Search` `Redux` `Client Side`
- [Redux Segment](https://github.com/rangle/redux-segment) - Segment.io analytics integration for Redux. Connect Redux actions to Segment analytics for tracking user behavior. ([Read more](/details/redux-segment.md)) `Analytics` `Segment` `Telemetry`
- [Redux Toolkit](https://redux-toolkit.js.org/) - The official, opinionated, batteries-included toolset for efficient Redux development. Simplifies Redux with less boilerplate, built-in Immer for immutable updates, and Redux Thunk for async logic. Includes powerful DevTools integration and TypeScript support. ([Read more](/details/redux-toolkit.md)) `Redux` `State` `Toolkit` `Async`
- [Reselect](https://github.com/reactjs/reselect) - Selector library for Redux. Provides composable, memoized selector functions for computing derived data from Redux store state. ([Read more](/details/reselect.md)) `Redux` `Memoization` `Selectors`
- [RTK Query](https://redux-toolkit.js.org/rtk-query/overview) - Official data fetching and caching tool from Redux Toolkit. Integrates seamlessly with Redux for applications already using Redux, providing automatic caching, deduplication, and real-time updates without needing a separate data fetching library. ([Read more](/details/rtk-query.md)) `Data Fetching` `Redux` `Caching`
- [Synergies](https://github.com/lukasbach/synergies) - A performant and distributed context-state library for creating reusable React state logic by synergizing atomic context pieces. ([Read more](/details/synergies.md)) `Context` `Distributed` `Reusable`
- [TComb React](https://github.com/gcanti/tcomb-react) - Alternative syntax for PropTypes in React applications. Provides a type-checking system built on tcomb for validating React component props. ([Read more](/details/tcomb-react.md)) `Type Checking` `propTypes` `Validation`
- [Teaful](https://github.com/teafuljs/teaful) - Tiny, easy and powerful React state management library. Provides a simple, hook-based API for managing application state with minimal boilerplate. ([Read more](/details/teaful.md)) `Minimal` `Hooks` `Lightweight`
- [Valtio](https://valtio.pmnd.rs/) - A minimal, proxy-based state management library for React where you can mutate state directly while keeping components reactive, praised for its simplicity. ([Read more](/details/valtio.md)) `Proxy` `Mutable` `Minimal`
- [XState](https://xstate.js.org/) - Finite state machines and statecharts for React, uniquely focused on managing complex application states with many states and transitions between them. ([Read more](/details/xstate.md)) `State Machines` `Statecharts` `Workflows`
- [Zustand](https://zustand.github.io/) - Zustand is a simple and lightweight state management library for React applications. It offers a clean API for managing global state without the need for context or complex setup, making it ideal for medium to large-scale React projects.
 ([Read more](/details/zustand.md)) `State Management` `React Hooks` `Minimalist`

## UI Animation

- [AOS - Animate On Scroll](https://michalsnik.github.io/aos/) - AOS (Animate On Scroll) is a lightweight, dependency-free JavaScript library that triggers CSS animations on elements as they enter the viewport during page scrolling. It's designed around performance, using CSS for animations and JavaScript only for scroll detection and triggering, keeping the gzipped footprint at just ~3.2KB. Key features include 50+ built-in animations (fade, flip, slide, zoom), easy declarative API using data attributes, customizable duration/delay/easing, and options for single or repeated triggering per scroll pass. Primary use cases include landing pages, marketing sites, portfolio websites, and product showcases that benefit from scroll-driven visual engagement. Compared to heavier libraries like wow.js (Animate.css companion) or Intersection Observer-based custom implementations, AOS offers a simpler setup with no external dependencies and better performance, though it lacks the advanced timeline control of ScrollTrigger (GSAP). ([Read more](/details/aos-animate-on-scroll.md)) `Scroll Animations` `Css Animations` `Lightweight`
- [AriaKit](https://ariakit.org/) - AriaKit is an open-source library of unstyled, accessible React component primitives that handle complex accessibility concerns like keyboard navigation, focus management, and WAI-ARIA attributes automatically. With over 20 components including buttons, dialogs, comboboxes, menus, tabs, and tooltips, it provides the behavioral foundation for building custom-styled interactive UIs. Primary use cases include building design systems, accessible enterprise applications, and custom component libraries. Compared to Radix UI (a direct competitor with similar headless approach), AriaKit offers more components including comboboxes and tables, while also supporting server components and providing built-in animation utilities. ([Read more](/details/ariakit.md)) `Accessibility` `WCAG` `Headless`
- [Base UI](https://mui.com/base-ui/) - Base UI is an unstyled, accessible React component library from the MUI team that provides foundational UI primitives with built-in WAI-ARIA compliance, focus management, and keyboard navigation. Rather than providing styled components, it delivers the behavioral and accessibility layer so developers can apply their own design system styling. Key features include a customizable slot system, hooks-based API for headless development, TypeScript-first design, and minimal bundle size. Primary use cases include building branded design systems, accessible enterprise applications, and custom component libraries. Compared to Radix UI or AriaKit, Base UI benefits from MUI's ecosystem and long-term support, while offering similar headless architecture. ([Read more](/details/base-ui.md)) `Unstyled` `Accessibility` `Design System`
- [Animate.css](https://animate.style) - Animate.css is a popular cross-browser CSS animation library providing 80+ pre-built, ready-to-use animations through simple class names. With over 80k GitHub stars, it covers categories like entrance/exit effects, attention seekers, bouncing, fading, flipping, rotation, sliding, and zoom animations. Key features include CSS custom properties for customization, animation delays and durations, and compatibility with JavaScript libraries or standalone use. Primary use cases include page transitions, scroll-triggered reveals, hover effects, and element emphasis in marketing sites and web apps. Compared to heavier JS animation libraries like GSAP, Animate.css is lightweight, requires no JavaScript, and is ideal for quick, common animations, though it lacks the complex timeline control and sequencing capabilities of JS-based alternatives. ([Read more](/details/animatecss.md)) `Css Animations` `Lightweight` `Predefined Effects`
- [Anime.js](https://animejs.com/) - Anime.js is a lightweight (~9KB gzipped) JavaScript animation library with a simple yet powerful API for animating CSS properties, SVG, DOM attributes, and JavaScript objects. It features timeline controls, keyframe support, stagger animations, and smooth easing functions. Primary use cases include UI micro-interactions, SVG motion graphics, loading animations, and interactive illustrations. Compared to GSAP (more feature-rich but larger), Anime.js offers a smaller footprint while still supporting complex multi-property animations and timeline sequencing. ([Read more](/details/animejs.md)) `Animation` `Svg` `Lightweight`
- [Auto Size Transition](https://github.com/renators/auto-size-transition) - Auto Size Transition is a React component library that dynamically measures and smoothly transitions containers to fit their content size, solving the common problem of animating height and width changes that browsers typically can't handle with CSS alone. It uses requestAnimationFrame-based measurement and interpolation for butter-smooth animations. Key features include zero-layout-thrashing measurement, support for nested animated transitions, configurable durations and easing functions, and support for both open/close and arbitrary content resize scenarios. Primary use cases include collapsible panels, expandable accordions, dropdown menus, and any UI where content height changes dynamically. Compared to CSS-only height: 0 → height: auto workarounds (which are limited and often buggy) or general-purpose animation libraries like Framer Motion (which don't specifically optimize for content-aware sizing), this component is purpose-built for this single task with optimized performance. ([Read more](/details/auto-size-transition.md)) `Animation` `Responsive` `Dynamic Sizing`
- [AutoAnimate](https://auto-animate.formkit.com/) - AutoAnimate is a zero-configuration animation library created by FormKit that automatically detects DOM additions, removals, and state changes to add smooth layout transitions with a single function call. It weighs only 1.5 KB gzipped and works by wrapping any parent element to animate its children's positional changes. Key features include zero-configuration setup (just add useAutoAnimate to any parent element), support for React hooks, automatic handling of conditional rendering and list reordering, and customizable durations and easing functions. Primary use cases include animating list additions/removals, accordion open/close transitions, tab panel switching, and conditional UI element reveals. Compared to Framer Motion (which requires explicit animate prop declarations) or CSS transitions (which can't animate DOM additions/removals), AutoAnimate provides the simplest path to adding motion to React applications with virtually no code changes. ([Read more](/details/autoanimate.md)) `Auto Animation` `Lightweight` `Zero Config`
- [Gooey React](https://gooey-react.netlify.app/) - Gooey React is a React component library that implements the gooey/blob effect using SVG filters, enabling organic, fluid-like metaball animations between elements. It creates visually striking shape-merging effects where nearby blobs appear to connect and flow together, commonly seen in creative websites and interactive art pieces.

**Key Features:**
- SVG filter-based gooey/blob effects for performance
- Metaball-style shape merging between nearby elements
- Smooth organic animations with CSS transitions
- Responsive design support
- Composable React components for easy integration
- Customizable blur and threshold values

**Primary Use Cases:** Creative landing pages, interactive art installations, animated logos, organic UI effects, and visually distinctive web experiences.

**Compared to Alternatives:** Unlike CSS-only blob effects (limited animation) or Canvas/WebGL approaches (complex setup), Gooey React provides a ready-to-use SVG filter solution that works declaratively within React's component model with minimal configuration. ([Read more](/details/gooey-react.md)) `Gooey` `Metaballs` `Svg Filter`
- [simpleParallax.js](https://github.com/geosigno/simpleParallax.js) - A lightweight and easy-to-use JavaScript library that adds parallax effects to images, with React support through simple integration. ([Read more](/details/simpleparallaxjs.md)) `Parallax` `Lightweight` `Image Effects`

Provides a large icon catalog with strong brand and social icon coverage, delivered as SVGs or web-font-based assets. ([Read more](/details/fontawesome-react.md)) `Icons` `Brand Icons` `Svg`
- [formkit/drag-and-drop](https://drag-and-drop.formkit.com/) - Lightweight, framework-agnostic drag-and-drop library with React and Vue wrappers that updates a reactive data model instead of directly manipulating the DOM. At approximately 5KB gzipped, it offers a simple, hook-based API for state-driven drag-and-drop interactions. ([Read more](/details/formkitdrag-and-drop.md)) `Drag And Drop` `Lightweight` `Reactive`
- [fullPage.js](https://alvarotrigo.com/fullPage/) - Full-screen scrolling library for React that enables building immersive single-page applications with vertical and horizontal slides. Ideal for storytelling, landing pages, and visually rich websites with touch, mouse wheel, and responsive design support. ([Read more](/details/fullpagejs.md)) `Full Screen` `Scrolling` `Responsive`
- [Gradient Picker](https://github.com/illyism/gradient-picker) - A React component for selecting solid colors, gradients, or background images, designed for seamless integration with the shadcn/ui ecosystem. Supports tabs for solid, gradient, and image selection modes. ([Read more](/details/gradient-picker.md)) `Gradient` `Color Picker` `Shadcn Compatible`
- [Hugeicons](https://hugeicons.com) - Production-ready icon library with 46,000+ icons in 10 styles, including 4,600+ free open-source icons in stroke-rounded style. Designed for modern SaaS products, dashboards, AI-driven interfaces, and design-driven applications. ([Read more](/details/hugeicons.md)) `Icons` `Design System` `Saas`

Supports multiple color spaces (Hex, HSL, RGB) and integrates with the shadcn/ui ecosystem via copy-and-paste installation. Integrates seamlessly with the MUI ecosystem for React applications. ([Read more](/details/mui-date-calendar.md)) `Enterprise` `Material Design` `Accessibility`
- [MUI-datatables](https://github.com/gregnb/mui-datatables) - A customizable data tables component for React built on top of Material-UI. ([Read more](/details/mui-datatables.md)) `Material Ui` `Data Table` `Open Source`
- [Notiflix](https://github.com/notiflix/Notiflix) - Powerful and feature-rich notification library providing dynamic notifications, loading indicators, and error alerts for web applications. Supports various notification types with extensive customization options for appearance and behavior. ([Read more](/details/notiflix.md)) `Notifications` `Loading Indicators` `Open Source`
- [qrcode.react](https://github.com/zpao/qrcode.react) - A React component for generating QR codes. Renders customizable QR codes as SVG elements in React applications. ([Read more](/details/qrcodereact.md)) `Qr Code` `Svg` `Generator`
- [Raily Dev Shadcn UI Customizer](https://customizer.railly.dev/) - A visual theme-customization tool for shadcn/ui that lets users change color tokens, typography, and design variables via interactive color pickers with live preview, producing ready-to-use themes. - [Rangeen](https://navnote.github.io/rangeen/) - An open-source color palette generator for shadcn/ui and Tailwind CSS projects. Helps developers pick colors, visualize palettes, and generate theme files for easy integration into UI systems. ([Read more](/details/rangeen.md)) `Open Source` `Color Palette` `Theme Generator`
- [rc-table](https://github.com/react-component/table) - Core table component from the react-component organization that powers Ant Design's Table. ## Boilerplate/Scaffolding

- [Nx](https://nx.dev) - Next generation build system with first class monorepo support and powerful integrations. Enables efficient development of scalable React applications in monorepos. ([Read more](/details/nx.md)) `Monorepo` `Build System` `Scalability`

- [AlignUI Pro](https://www.alignui.com/) - AlignUI Pro is a premium React admin dashboard and component library built with Tailwind CSS, Radix UI, and React Aria. It offers a comprehensive collection of professionally designed components, dashboard layouts, and full-page templates for enterprise business applications. The product ships with a matching Figma design system and includes components for charts, data tables, forms, authentication flows, and complete admin page layouts. Primary use cases include SaaS admin panels, internal dashboards, and enterprise applications that require polished, production-ready UI. Compared to free alternatives like open-source admin templates, AlignUI Pro provides a unified, cohesive design language with ongoing support, though it requires a paid license and has a smaller community. ([Read more](/details/alignui-pro.md)) `Premium` `Tailwind Css` `Admin Dashboard`
- [Argon Dashboard](https://github.com/creativetimofficial/nextjs-argon-dashboard) - Argon Dashboard is a free, open-source Next.js admin dashboard template built with Bootstrap components and Chart.js for data visualization. It provides a clean, modern UI with pre-built admin pages, charts, and user management screens designed for rapid development of analytics-oriented applications. Key features include responsive Bootstrap 4/5 layouts, multiple chart types with Chart.js, user authentication pages, profile and settings screens, and a cohesive design language inspired by Google's Material Design. Primary use cases include admin panels, analytics dashboards, CRM systems, and data-driven web applications requiring a polished, out-of-the-box admin interface. Compared to premium alternatives like Creative Tim's Argon Pro or other commercial dashboards, the free version offers a solid starting point with fewer pages and components, while compared to custom-built admin panels, it significantly reduces development time for standard admin use cases. ([Read more](/details/argon-dashboard.md)) `Next.js` `Bootstrap` `Admin Dashboard`

It includes multiple chart libraries with visualizations, data tables, forms, calendars, profile pages, and authentication screens. Key features include Material Design-compliant components, multiple dashboard variants with charts and KPIs, extensive user management pages, built-in calendar and email UIs, form validation, and Figma design files (premium). Primary use cases include admin backends, analytics dashboards, CRM systems, and enterprise applications needing a Material Design-based starting point. Compared to alternatives like CoreUI or Argon Dashboard (which use Bootstrap), Berry leverages MUI for a more polished but opinionated look, though its strict adherence to Material Design may feel dated compared to modern flat design trends seen in Tailwind-based templates like shadcn/ui. ([Read more](/details/berry.md)) `Material Ui` `Admin Dashboard` `React Template`

- [PBandJ](https://github.com/moishinetzer/pbandj) - PBandJ is a zero-configuration, reusable component framework that provides a streamlined setup for creating shareable React component libraries without the complexity of manual build tooling. It simplifies the scaffolding, building, and bundling process for component development by handling configuration automatically while supporting modern JavaScript features and TypeScript out of the box. Key features include zero-configuration setup that eliminates webpack and Babel boilerplate, automatic component bundling with tree-shaking support for optimal delivery, built-in Storybook integration for component documentation and visual testing, TypeScript support with automatic type definition generation, multiple output formats (CommonJS, ESM, UMD) for universal compatibility, and hot module reloading during development for rapid iteration. Primary use cases include building internal design systems that need to be shared across multiple projects, creating open-source component libraries with minimal tooling overhead, and teams wanting to extract reusable components from monolithic applications into publishable packages. Compared to manual configuration with Create React App or custom webpack setups, PBandJ provides a convention-over-configuration approach specifically designed for component library development. - [Rockpack](https://github.com/AlexSergey/rockpack) - Rockpack is a zero-configuration build tool and bundler for React applications that provides an opinionated setup for development, production builds, server-side rendering (SSR), linting, and testing — all configured out of the box. It wraps webpack, Babel, and other tooling into a simplified CLI interface, enabling developers to create production-ready React apps in minutes without managing complex build configurations. Key features include zero-configuration setup with sensible defaults, server-side rendering support for SEO-friendly applications, built-in development server with hot module replacement, production bundling with code splitting and tree shaking, integrated linting and testing tooling, and multiple webpack plugins pre-configured for React optimization. Primary use cases include rapid prototyping, small team projects that need a working React app quickly, and developers who want webpack-powered builds without writing webpack.config.js files. Compared to Create React App (which lacks SSR support and is now in maintenance mode) or Vite (faster but less integrated), Rockpack focuses on simplicity and convention over configuration specifically tailored for React projects. ([Read more](/details/rockpack.md)) `SSR` `Bundling` `Zero Config`

## Code Display

- [Monaco Editor for React](https://monaco-react.surenatoyan.com/) - Monaco Editor component for React based on the Microsoft Visual Studio Code editor. - [React Key Handler](https://github.com/ayrton/react-key-handler) - React Key Handler is a declarative keyboard event handling library that maps key presses and key combinations directly to component behaviors, eliminating the need for manual event listener attachment and cleanup. It provides focus-aware event targeting so key handlers only fire when their associated components are active. Key features include declarative key-to-behavior mapping through a clean API, focus-aware event targeting that prevents global conflicts, support for single keys and key sequences (e.g., Ctrl+K), automatic cleanup of event listeners on unmount to prevent memory leaks, and composable API design that works alongside other React component patterns. Primary use cases include keyboard shortcuts for power users, accessible menu navigation, hotkey-driven workflows in IDE-like applications, and any interface where keyboard interaction improves productivity. Compared to react-hotkeys-hook or @reach/skip-nav (which focus on single-purpose scenarios), React Key Handler offers a more flexible, declarative mapping system for complex keyboard-driven interfaces. ## 3D Visualization

- [React Three Fiber](https://docs.pmnd.rs/react-three-fiber/) - A React renderer for Three.js that brings declarative, reactive, and component-based patterns to 3D rendering. Build 3D scenes in React with all the power of Three.js. ([Read more](/details/react-three-fiber.md)) `3D` `Three.js` `Graphics`
- [A-Frame React](https://github.com/ngokevin/aframe-react) - A-Frame React provides React bindings for A-Frame's WebVR/WebXR framework, enabling developers to build immersive 3D and virtual reality web applications using familiar React component patterns. It bridges A-Frame's entity-component system with React's declarative JSX, allowing VR scenes to be composed as React component trees. Key features include declarative 3D scene composition using React components, React lifecycle integration for A-Frame entities, support for VR headsets and mobile AR experiences, event handling between React and A-Frame systems, and TypeScript type definitions. Primary use cases include VR exhibitions, 3D product visualizations, interactive educational experiences, virtual showrooms, and gamified web content. Compared to React Three Fiber (which offers more granular control over Three.js rendering with a React-first API), A-Frame React is simpler to get started with and better suited for VR-specific use cases, though it provides less flexibility for custom 3D rendering pipelines. ([Read more](/details/aframe-react.md)) `Virtual Reality` `A Frame` `Webvr`
- [React Three Drei](https://github.com/pmndrs/drei) - A collection of useful helpers and abstractions for React Three Fiber. Provides ready-to-use components for cameras, controls, shapes, and effects to accelerate 3D development. ([Read more](/details/react-three-drei.md)) `3D` `Three.js` `Helpers`

## Authentication

- [React Apple Signin Auth](https://github.com/A-Tokyo/react-apple-signin-auth) - Apple Sign In component for React using the official Apple JS SDK. Provides native Apple authentication flow integration with customizable button styling. ([Read more](/details/react-apple-signin-auth.md)) `Apple` `Oauth` `Signin`
- [Auth0](https://auth0.com/) - Auth0 (now part of Okta) is an enterprise-grade authentication and identity management platform that provides drop-in authentication for web and mobile applications through Universal Login, Social Identity Providers, and enterprise protocols including OAuth 2.0, OIDC, and SAML. It handles complex authentication flows, MFA, passwordless login, and user management. Key features include customizable Universal Login with hosted pages, 100+ social and enterprise identity providers, Multi-Factor Authentication with push, SMS, and authenticator apps, role-based access control with custom claims and rules, advanced threat detection with anomaly alerts, and SDKs for every major platform including React. Primary use cases include enterprise applications, SaaS platforms, B2B products requiring SSO, and any application requiring secure, production-ready authentication without building it from scratch. Compared to open-source alternatives like Auth.js (self-hosted, more limited features), Auth0 provides managed security compliance, SOC 2 certification, and enterprise features at the cost of usage-based pricing. ([Read more](/details/auth0.md)) `Authentication` `Identity` `Oauth`
- [AuthKit](https://www.authkit.com/) - AuthKit is a streamlined authentication solution for web applications that provides sign-up, sign-in, password recovery, and session management functionality through a developer-friendly API. Key features include OAuth provider integration, customizable auth flows, passwordless authentication options, and built-in security protections. Primary use cases include SaaS applications, membership sites, and any React app needing user authentication. Compared to Auth0 (enterprise-focused, pricier at scale) and Auth.js (open-source, self-hosted), AuthKit positions itself as a balanced option offering ease of use without the complexity of enterprise platforms or the self-hosting requirements of open-source alternatives. ([Read more](/details/authkit.md)) `Authentication` `User Management` `Identity`
- [Better Auth](https://www.better-auth.com/) - Better Auth is a modern, framework-agnostic, type-safe authentication library designed for full-stack JavaScript and TypeScript applications. It provides a comprehensive authentication solution with support for OAuth providers, email/password authentication, magic links, multi-factor authentication, and session management with a developer-first API. Key features include full type safety with TypeScript inference, framework-agnostic design working with React, Next.js, SvelteKit, and others, database adapters for multiple backends, email verification, password reset flows, and built-in security protections including CSRF and rate limiting. Primary use cases include SaaS applications, membership platforms, internal tools, and any full-stack app needing production-ready authentication. Compared to Auth.js (formerly NextAuth.js, which is Next.js-centric) or proprietary solutions like Auth0 (hosted, per-user pricing), Better Auth offers open-source self-hosted authentication with broader framework support and more granular control over auth flows. ([Read more](/details/better-auth.md)) `Authentication` `Type Safe` `Framework Agnostic`
- [Iron Session](https://github.com/vvo/iron-session) - Iron Session is a secure, stateless, cookie-based session library for Node.js and Next.js that encrypts session data directly within cookies using the Iron encryption library, eliminating the need for server-side session storage. It provides a simple, type-safe API for creating and managing encrypted sessions in server-side React applications.

**Key Features:**
- Encrypted cookie sessions using battle-tested Iron encryption
- Stateless architecture requiring no database or Redis
- Seamless Next.js App Router and Pages Router integration
- TypeScript-first design with full type inference
- Automatic session rotation and expiration handling
- Works with any Node.js server (Express, Fastify, etc.)

**Primary Use Cases:** Next.js authentication flows, session-based user state in serverless environments, simple login systems without database overhead, and edge-compatible session management.

**Compared to Alternatives:** Unlike express-session or next-session which store sessions server-side (requiring Redis or database), iron-session stores everything encrypted in cookies, making it serverless-friendly and simpler to deploy. However, it's limited by cookie size (~4KB) compared to server-side approaches that can store arbitrary amounts of data. ([Read more](/details/iron-session.md)) `Session` `Cookies` `Encryption`

Designed to speed up builds by caching previous build outputs and executing tasks in parallel, making monorepo management seamless for React projects. ## Carousels & Sliders

- [Swiper](https://swiperjs.com) - Modern open-source JavaScript carousel and slider library with React wrapper, supporting mobile touch gestures, hardware-accelerated transitions, and used by Netflix and Adobe. ([Read more](/details/swiper.md)) `Carousel` `Slider` `Touch Friendly`
- [Embla Carousel React](https://www.embla-carousel.com) - A lightweight carousel library with fluid motion and swipe precision, providing a smooth scrolling experience with React hooks and extensive plugin support. ([Read more](/details/embla-carousel-react.md)) `Carousel` `Slider` `Lightweight` `Fluid`
- [Glide.js](https://glidejs.com/) - Glide.js is a lightweight, dependency-free JavaScript ES6 slider and carousel library that delivers touch-enabled, responsive carousels at just ~7KB gzipped with zero external dependencies. It supports multiple slider modes including carousel, rewind, and peek, with smooth GPU-accelerated animations and built-in accessibility support. Key features include three slider modes — carousel (infinite loop), slider (rewind), and peek (show partial slides) for flexible layout needs, zero dependencies keeping bundle size at just ~7KB gzipped, full touch and swipe gesture support for mobile devices, keyboard navigation with arrow key control and ARIA attributes for accessibility, breakpoints API for responsive behavior changes at different screen sizes, and a modular architecture allowing selective inclusion of only the components you need (autoplay, controls, keyboard, swipe, anchors). Primary use cases include product image galleries, hero section carousels, testimonial rotators, portfolio displays, and content sliders. Compared to heavier alternatives like Swiper (more features but 30+ KB) or Slick Carousel (requires jQuery), Glide.js offers the best balance of features, performance, and zero-dependency simplicity for projects needing a fast, lightweight carousel. ([Read more](/details/glidejs.md)) `Carousel` `Slider` `Lightweight`
- [Keen Slider](https://keen-slider.io/) - A lightweight, performance-focused slider library with no dependencies, offering smooth touch interactions and extensive customization for modern web applications. ([Read more](/details/keen-slider.md)) `Carousel` `Lightweight` `Performance`
- [Keen Slider React](https://keen-slider.io) - A lightweight, framework-agnostic carousel library with React bindings, offering smooth animations, touch gestures, and minimal footprint for modern web applications. ([Read more](/details/keen-slider-react.md)) `Carousel` `Slider` `Lightweight` `Touch`
- [Nuka Carousel](https://github.com/FormidableLabs/nuka-carousel) - A small, fast, and accessibility-first React carousel library developed by Formidable Labs, featuring custom animations and zero dependencies. ([Read more](/details/nuka-carousel.md)) `Carousel` `Accessible` `Formidable`
- [Pure React Carousel](https://www.npmjs.com/package/pure-react-carousel) - A fully controlled, responsive React carousel component with 100% test coverage, allowing flexible DOM order and complete customization without external dependencies. ([Read more](/details/pure-react-carousel.md)) `Carousel` `Controlled` `Responsive`
- [React Carousel Slider](https://github.com/brillout/react-carousel-slider) - Responsive image and content carousel with autoplay, swipe gestures, and customizable navigation for React applications. ([Read more](/details/react-carousel-slider.md)) `Open Source` `Carousel` `Slideshow`
- [React Image Gallery](https://github.com/xiaolin/react-image-gallery) - Image gallery and carousel component for React with full-screen lightbox support. Provides customizable image galleries with thumbnail navigation and various display modes. ([Read more](/details/react-image-gallery.md)) `Gallery` `Carousel` `Lightbox`
- [React Multi Carousel](https://www.npmjs.com/package/react-multi-carousel) - A production-ready, lightweight React carousel component with SSR support, responsive breakpoints, and excellent mobile touch interactions. ([Read more](/details/react-multi-carousel.md)) `Carousel` `Responsive` `SSR`
- [React Responsive Carousel](https://www.npmjs.com/package/react-responsive-carousel) - A dynamic and flexible carousel component that seamlessly adapts to different screen sizes with lazy loading support and hardware-accelerated transitions. ([Read more](/details/react-responsive-carousel.md)) `Carousel` `Responsive` `Lazy Loading`
- [React Slick](https://react-slick.neostack.com) - Carousel component for React applications offering responsive and customizable carousels with transition effects, autoplay settings, navigation buttons, and pagination controls. ([Read more](/details/react-slick.md)) `Carousel` `Slider` `Responsive`
- [React Tiny Slider](https://github.com/nerdyman/react-tiny-slider) - React wrapper for Tiny Slider, a lightweight carousel/slider component. Provides responsive carousel functionality with touch support and minimal configuration. ([Read more](/details/react-tiny-slider.md)) `Carousel` `Slider` `Responsive`
- [Splide](https://splidejs.com/) - A lightweight, flexible, and accessible slider and carousel library with no dependencies, written in TypeScript with extensive customization options. ([Read more](/details/splide.md)) `Carousel` `Slider` `Accessible`
- [Tiny Slider](https://github.com/ganlanyuan/tiny-slider) - A vanilla JavaScript slider that works with all browsers, extremely lightweight at 10kb gzipped, with no dependencies and excellent performance. ([Read more](/details/tiny-slider.md)) `Carousel` `Vanilla Js` `Lightweight`

## CSS/Styling

- [Styled Components](https://github.com/styled-components/styled-components) - Visual primitives for the component age. A CSS-in-JS library for React that allows writing CSS directly inside JavaScript components with tagged template literals. ([Read more](/details/styled-components.md)) `Css In Js` `Tagged Templates` `Theming`
- [Aphrodite](https://github.com/Khan/aphrodite) - Aphrodite is a framework-agnostic CSS-in-JS library developed by Khan Academy that automatically handles vendor prefixing, style deduplication, and critical CSS extraction for React and other applications. It provides a clean API for writing inline styles in JavaScript while generating efficient CSS output at runtime. Key features include automatic vendor prefixing for cross-browser compatibility, server-side rendering support with critical CSS extraction, style deduplication to minimize output, and production minification. Primary use cases include React component styling, universal/isomorphic applications requiring SSR, and projects needing a simple CSS-in-JS solution without heavy runtime overhead. Compared to styled-components or Emotion (which offer more features like theming and css prop), Aphrodite is simpler and lighter, though less feature-rich. ([Read more](/details/aphrodite.md)) `Css In Js` `Inline Styles` `Vendor Prefixing`
- [ClassmateJS React](https://github.com/richard-unterberg/classmatejs/tree/master/packages/react) - A class name focused component builder with a syntax like styled components and the sugar of CVA's variants. Part of the ClassmateJS ecosystem. ([Read more](/details/classmatejs-react.md)) `Class Names` `Variational` `Styled Components Like`
- [Emotion](https://emotion.sh/) - CSS-in-JS library for React that enables writing styles using JavaScript template literals or object styles. An alternative to styled-components with support for both the styled pattern and the css prop for co-locating styles with components. ([Read more](/details/emotion.md)) `Css In Js` `Styling` `Styled`
- [Flexoki](https://github.com/kepano/flexoki) - An inky, analog-inspired color scheme designed for reading and writing on digital screens. Provides both light and dark variants with CSS variables, optimized for prose and code editors. ([Read more](/details/flexoki.md)) `Color Palette` `Dark Mode` `Typography`
- [Inline Style Prefixer](https://github.com/rofrischmann/inline-style-prefixer) - Run-time Autoprefixer for Inline Style Objects. Automatically adds vendor prefixes to inline styles for cross-browser compatibility. ([Read more](/details/inline-style-prefixer.md)) `Autoprefixer` `Vendor Prefixing` `Inline Styles`
- [Isomorphic Style Loader](https://github.com/kriasoft/isomorphic-style-loader) - Isomorphic CSS style loader for Webpack. Enables server-side rendering of CSS styles with critical CSS extraction. ([Read more](/details/isomorphic-style-loader.md)) `Webpack` `Isomorphic` `Critical Css`
- [Linaria](https://linaria.dev/) - Zero-runtime CSS-in-JS library for React that compiles styles at build time. Combines the developer experience of CSS-in-JS with the performance of static CSS, enabling standard CSS syntax in JavaScript with full server-side rendering support. ([Read more](/details/linaria.md)) `Css In Js` `Zero Runtime` `Compiled`
- [PandaCSS](https://panda-css.com/) - Modern CSS-in-JS engine that compiles to atomic CSS at build time. Provides utility-first styling with type safety, conditional styling, recipes, and design token support, offering a zero-runtime CSS solution for React applications. ([Read more](/details/pandacss.md)) `Css In Js` `Atomic Css` `Type Safe`
- [React Container Query](https://github.com/d6u/react-container-query) - Modular responsive component for React that enables container-based queries. Allows components to respond to their own size rather than the viewport. ([Read more](/details/react-container-query.md)) `Container Queries` `Responsive` `Modular`
- [Reactponsive](https://github.com/jmlweb/reactponsive) - Responsive components and hooks for React. Provides utilities for building responsive UIs with component-level responsiveness. ([Read more](/details/reactponsive.md)) `Responsive` `Hooks` `Components`
- [Stitches](https://github.com/stitchesjs/stitches) - CSS-in-JS with near-zero runtime, SSR, and multi-variant support. A lightweight styling solution with excellent developer experience. ([Read more](/details/stitches.md)) `Css In Js` `Near Zero Runtime` `Multi Variant`
- [StyleX](https://stylexjs.com/) - CSS-in-JS styling library by Facebook that compiles to utility-first CSS at build time. Provides type-safe, fast React styling with colocation benefits without runtime overhead, addressing performance and hydration issues of traditional CSS-in-JS solutions. ([Read more](/details/stylex.md)) `Css In Js` `Compiled` `Facebook`
- [UnoCSS](https://unocss.dev/) - Instant, highly customizable atomic CSS engine inspired by Tailwind CSS and Windi CSS. Provides a fast, on-demand alternative to traditional CSS frameworks with full support for React applications and custom configurations. ([Read more](/details/unocss.md)) `Atomic Css` `Utility First` `Instant`
- [Vanilla Extract](https://vanilla-extract.style/) - TypeScript-first CSS styling engine with zero runtime. Offers compile-time CSS generation with features like theming, responsive utilities, and recipes, addressing the hydration and performance issues of traditional CSS-in-JS approaches. ([Read more](/details/vanilla-extract.md)) `Css In Ts` `Zero Runtime` `Type Safe`

## Dev Tools

- [Awesome React](https://github.com/enaqx/awesome-react) - Awesome React is a comprehensive, free directory of React ecosystem tools, libraries, frameworks, components, and resources with over 50,000+ GitHub stars, serving as the most referenced discovery resource in the React community. It covers everything from UI component libraries and state management solutions to testing frameworks, learning resources, tutorials, and developer tools. Key features include organization into dozens of detailed categories, community-maintained entries with links to repositories and documentation, and regular updates as the React ecosystem evolves. Primary use cases include discovering React libraries for new projects, exploring the full breadth of available solutions, and finding learning resources and tutorials. Compared to npm search (raw, uncurated results) or React Directory (more limited scope), Awesome React offers the most comprehensive human-curated overview of the entire React ecosystem. ([Read more](/details/awesome-react.md)) `Open Source` `Curated List` `React Ecosystem`
- [Babel Plugin React Remove PropTypes](https://github.com/oliviertassinari/babel-plugin-transform-react-remove-prop-types) - Babel Plugin Transform React Remove PropTypes is a build-time optimization tool that automatically strips React PropTypes definitions from production bundles, typically reducing bundle size by 2-10% depending on the codebase. It operates during Babel's compilation phase, meaning zero runtime overhead.

**Key Features:**
- Automatic PropTypes removal in production builds only
- Maintains PropTypes during development for full error checking
- Configurable ignore patterns to preserve specific PropTypes
- Supports both class and function components
- Integrates seamlessly with create-react-app and custom Babel configs
- Zero runtime cost since removal happens at compile time

**Primary Use Cases:** Production applications using PropTypes for development-time type checking that want to minimize bundle size. Ideal for large React apps with extensive PropTypes definitions.

**Compared to Alternatives:** Unlike TypeScript (which provides compile-time checking without any runtime or build-size cost), PropTypes add runtime overhead. This plugin gives you the best of both worlds: PropTypes during development, zero weight in production. ([Read more](/details/babel-plugin-react-remove-proptypes.md)) `Babel Plugin` `Optimization` `Bundle Size`
- [Biome](https://biomejs.dev/) - Fast, all-in-one toolchain for JavaScript and TypeScript projects written in Rust. Aims to replace both ESLint and Prettier by combining linting, formatting, and more into a single, high-performance tool with minimal setup. ([Read more](/details/biome.md)) `Linting` `Formatting` `Rust Based`
- [Component Controls](https://github.com/ccontrols/component-controls) - Component Controls is a documentation and testing tool for React component libraries that generates interactive documentation sites with live playgrounds, props tables, and visual regression testing. It provides a Storybook-like experience with MDX support, automatic prop documentation from TypeScript definitions, and built-in testing utilities.

**Key Features:**
- Interactive component playgrounds with live editing
- Automatic prop documentation from TypeScript/PropTypes
- MDX support for rich documentation pages
- Visual regression testing integration
- Theme switching and responsive preview modes
- Snapshot and unit test generation

**Primary Use Cases:** Design system documentation, component library development, UI regression testing, and creating self-documenting component showcases for development teams.

**Compared to Alternatives:** Unlike Storybook (the industry standard with massive ecosystem), Component Controls offers tighter TypeScript integration and built-in visual regression testing, but has a smaller community and fewer addons. ([Read more](/details/component-controls.md)) `Documentation` `Playground` `Component Library`
- [Cosmos](https://github.com/ghengeveld/cosmos) - Developer Experience (DX) tool for designing truly encapsulated React components. Provides an isolated playground for developing and testing components in isolation. ([Read more](/details/cosmos.md)) `Component Dev` `Playground` `DX`
- [DataFormsJS](https://github.com/dataformsjs/dataformsjs/blob/master/docs/jsx-loader.md) - Small JavaScript Compiler for quickly converting JSX to JS directly on a web page. Part of the DataFormsJS framework for building web applications. ([Read more](/details/dataformsjs.md)) `JSX` `Compiler` `Browser`
- [ESLint](https://eslint.org/) - Widely adopted linting utility for JavaScript and TypeScript that enforces consistent code style and catches potential errors. Essential tool in every React developer's workflow for maintaining code quality and following best practices. ([Read more](/details/eslint.md)) `Linting` `Code Quality` `Developer Experience`
- [FluxGuard](https://fluxguard.com) - Production change monitoring tool that highlights all DOM and design changes. Helps ensure UI consistency by detecting unintended visual changes. ([Read more](/details/fluxguard.md)) `Monitoring` `DOM-changes` `Visual Testing`
- [HTML to React Components](https://github.com/roman01la/html-to-react-components) - Extract annotated portions of HTML into React components as separate modules. Converts HTML markup into standalone React component files. ([Read more](/details/html-to-react-components.md)) `HTML-conversion` `Extraction` `Migration`
- [htmltojsx](https://github.com/reactjs/react-magic) - htmltojsx (part of the React Magic project) is a developer tool that converts plain HTML markup into React JSX components, enabling seamless migration of legacy websites and templates to the React ecosystem. It parses HTML attributes, class names, and inline styles, transforming them into their JSX equivalents including camelCased attributes and className conversions. Key features include automatic HTML-to-JSX syntax conversion, handling of inline style object generation from CSS strings, conversion of event handler attributes to React synthetic events, and command-line interface for batch processing existing templates. Primary use cases include migrating legacy HTML pages to React, converting designer handoff markup into React components, and rapidly prototyping JSX from existing HTML templates. Compared to manual conversion (time-consuming and error-prone) or online converters (limited in scope), htmltojsx provides programmatic conversion that can be integrated into build pipelines and migration scripts. ([Read more](/details/htmltojsx.md)) `HTML-conversion` `JSX` `Migration`
- [Jest](https://jestjs.io/) - JavaScript testing framework maintained by Meta that provides a test runner, assertion library, mocking, and code coverage. Widely used for unit and integration testing in React applications. ([Read more](/details/jest.md)) `Testing` `Unit Testing` `Mocking`
- [jsonx](https://github.com/repetere/jsonx) - React JSON Syntax. Render React components using only JSON, enabling data-driven UI generation from JSON definitions. ([Read more](/details/jsonx.md)) `JSON` `Syntax` `Data Driven`
- [Plasmic](https://www.plasmic.app/) - Powerful design tool for building React components visually. Enables designers and developers to collaborate on building UI components in a visual editor. ([Read more](/details/plasmic.md)) `Visual Editor` `No Code` `Design Tool`
- [React Demo Tab CLI](https://github.com/mkosir/react-demo-tab-cli) - CLI tool for creating interactive demos of React components. Generate standalone demo applications from component source files. ([Read more](/details/react-demo-tab-cli.md)) `Cli` `Demos` `Component Showcase`
- [React Device Frameset](https://github.com/zheeeng/react-device-frameset) - React device frameset component for displaying content within device mockups. - [Reactotron](https://github.com/infinitered/reactotron) - A cross-platform app for inspecting your React JS and React Native apps. Provides a visual interface for debugging state, API requests, and application behavior. ([Read more](/details/reactotron.md)) `Debugging` `Inspection` `React Native`

([Read more](/details/redux-devtools-chart-monitor.md)) `Redux` `Devtools` `Chart`
- [Redux DevTools Dock Monitor](https://github.com/reduxjs/redux-devtools) - A resizable and movable dock for Redux DevTools monitors. Allows developers to position, resize, and toggle the visibility of Redux DevTools with keyboard shortcuts. ([Read more](/details/redux-devtools-dock-monitor.md)) `Redux` `Devtools` `Monitor`
- [Redux DevTools Inspector](https://github.com/alexkuz/redux-devtools-inspector) - Another Redux DevTools Monitor providing a tree view for inspecting actions and state changes with filtering capabilities and action details. ([Read more](/details/redux-devtools-inspector.md)) `Redux` `Devtools` `Inspector`
- [Redux DevTools Remote](https://github.com/zalmoxisus/remote-redux-devtools) - Redux DevTools remotely provides the ability to connect Redux DevTools across different windows or devices, enabling remote debugging of Redux applications. ([Read more](/details/remote-redux-devtools.md)) `Redux` `Remote Debugging` `Devtools`
- [Redux Test Recorder](https://github.com/conorhastings/redux-test-recorder) - A Redux middleware to automatically generate tests for reducers through UI interaction. Records actions dispatched during interaction and generates corresponding unit tests. ([Read more](/details/redux-test-recorder.md)) `Redux` `Testing` `Auto Generate`
- [RUT](https://github.com/milesj/rut) - React testing made easy with react-test-renderer. Supports DOM and custom renderers, providing a clean abstraction for testing React components. ([Read more](/details/rut.md)) `Testing` `React Test Renderer` `Renderers`

## Form Management

- [React Hook Form](https://react-hook-form.com) - Performant, flexible form library using uncontrolled components and ref-based field registration to minimize re-renders, offering a clean API with optional validation schema support. ([Read more](/details/react-hook-form.md)) `Forms` `Validation` `Performance`
- [Formik](https://formik.org) - Popular form management library handling field values, validation, errors, and submission with reduced boilerplate and tedious form wiring in React applications. ([Read more](/details/formik.md)) `Forms` `Validation` `State Management`
- [React Final Form](https://final-form.org/react) - High-performance subscription-based form state management tool for React with small bundle size, allowing fine-grained control over field observation and re-renders. ([Read more](/details/react-final-form.md)) `Forms` `State Management` `Performance`
- [React Hook Form DevTools](https://react-hook-form.com/dev-tools) - A development tool component for React Hook Form that visualizes form state, validation errors, and field values in real-time, making form debugging effortless. ([Read more](/details/react-hook-form-devtools.md)) `Forms` `Devtools` `Debugging` `React Hook Form`
- [React JSON Schema Form](https://github.com/rjsf-team/react-jsonschema-form) - Build React forms automatically from JSON Schema. Generates form UI, validation, and submission handlers from schema definitions. ([Read more](/details/react-jsonschema-form.md)) `Forms` `JSON Schema` `Auto Generation`
- [React Step Wizard](https://github.com/jcmcneal/react-step-wizard) - Flexible multi-step wizard for React with custom transitions and hash-enabled navigation. Each child component becomes an individual step with built-in navigation controls. ([Read more](/details/react-step-wizard.md)) `Wizard` `Multi Step` `Forms`
- [TanStack Form](https://tanstack.com/form/latest) - A headless, performant, and type-safe form state management library for React, created by the team behind TanStack Table and TanStack Query, supporting complex validation and async operations. ([Read more](/details/tanstack-form.md)) `Forms` `Validation` `Typescript` `Headless`
- [Valibot](https://valibot.dev) - A modular, type-safe schema validation library optimized for bundle size, offering an alternative to Zod with better tree-shaking and smaller footprint for React applications. ([Read more](/details/valibot.md)) `Validation` `Typescript` `Schema` `Lightweight`
- [Yup](https://github.com/jquense/yup) - A JavaScript schema validation library for runtime value parsing and validation, widely used with Formik and React Hook Form for building complex form validation rules. ([Read more](/details/yup.md)) `Validation` `Forms` `Schema` `Javascript`
- [Zod](https://zod.dev) - A TypeScript-first schema validation library with static type inference, providing runtime validation with excellent developer experience and seamless integration with React form libraries. ([Read more](/details/zod.md)) `Validation` `Typescript` `Schema` `Type Safety`

## Framework Integrations

- [React Native](https://reactnative.dev/) - Facebook's framework for building native mobile applications using React. Enables developers to use React's component-based architecture to create cross-platform mobile apps for iOS and Android with a single codebase. ([Read more](/details/react-native.md)) `Mobile` `Cross Platform` `Native`
- [Backbone React Component](https://github.com/magalhas/backbone-react-component) - Backbone React Component is a minimal integration library that bridges Backbone.js models and collections with React components, automatically syncing state changes and triggering re-renders when underlying data mutates. It provides a thin wrapper around React's lifecycle methods to bind Backbone events seamlessly. Key features include automatic model/collection binding, mixin-based integration with React components, automatic cleanup of event listeners on unmount, and support for both individual models and collections. Primary use cases include legacy applications migrating from Backbone to React incrementally, projects that use Backbone on the client side but want React for the view layer, and teams needing to maintain both frameworks during transition periods. Compared to modern state management solutions like Redux or Zustand, this is primarily a compatibility bridge for existing Backbone codebases rather than a recommended approach for new projects. ([Read more](/details/backbone-react-component.md)) `Backbone` `Model Binding` `Integration`
- [Electron](https://www.electronjs.org/) - Mature framework for building cross-platform desktop applications using web technologies. Bundles Chromium and Node.js, enabling React developers to create desktop apps with full access to native operating system APIs. ([Read more](/details/electron.md)) `Desktop` `Cross Platform` `Nodejs`
- [Elm React Component](https://github.com/KtorZ/elm-react-component) - A React component which wraps an Elm module to be used in a React application. Enables integration of Elm programs within React component trees. ([Read more](/details/elm-react-component.md)) `Elm` `Interop` `Wrapping`
- [Expo](https://expo.dev/) - The most popular framework for creating React Native applications. Provides a comprehensive toolchain for building, deploying, and managing cross-platform mobile apps with simplified native module integration and over-the-air updates. ([Read more](/details/expo.md)) `Mobile` `React Native` `Cross Platform`
- [gl-react](https://github.com/nicknisi/gl-react) - OpenGL/WebGL bindings for React to implement complex effects over images and content. Enables GPU-accelerated graphics in React applications. ([Read more](/details/gl-react.md)) `OpenGL` `WebGL` `Graphics`
- [React Backbon](https://github.com/jhudson8/react-backbone) - Backbone-aware mixins for React and more. Provides integration between Backbone and React with data synchronization capabilities. ([Read more](/details/react-backbon.md)) `Backbone` `Mixins` `Integration`
- [React D3 Library](https://github.com/react-d3-library/react-d3-library) - Open source library for using D3 in React. Bridges the gap between D3's data visualization capabilities and React's component model. ([Read more](/details/react-d3-library.md)) `D3` `Data Visualization` `Charts`
- [React Elm Components](https://github.com/evancz/react-elm-components) - React Elm Components is a small utility library by Evan Czaplicki (creator of the Elm programming language) that enables embedding Elm programs as React components. It provides a bridge between React's component model and Elm's pure functional architecture through the Elm Architecture pattern. Key features include seamless integration of Elm programs within React component trees, automatic port communication between React and Elm, simple render props for embedding Elm views, and a clean API for sending commands and receiving subscriptions from React. Primary use cases include incrementally migrating existing React applications to Elm, embedding Elm modules within larger React applications, and teams wanting to leverage Elm's strong type safety and runtime guarantees for specific UI modules. Compared to full Elm applications, this allows gradual adoption, though it has largely been superseded as Elm's momentum declined in favor of TypeScript with React. ([Read more](/details/react-elm-components.md)) `Elm` `Integration` `Components`
- [React Famous](https://github.com/pilwon/react-famous) - React Famous is a bridge library that enables integration of Famo.us — a high-performance WebGL/3D rendering engine — with React's component model. It allows developers to embed Famo.us's performant 3D transforms and physics-based animations within React component trees. Key features include 3D CSS transforms and WebGL rendering directly within React components, a layout engine that uses CSS transforms instead of layout reflows for performance, and integration of Famo.us physics and gesture systems with React's declarative API. Primary use cases included 3D user interfaces, physics-based animations, parallax scrolling effects, and high-performance mobile UIs. Note: Famo.us was discontinued as a standalone project around 2016, making this a historical/archival library rather than an active recommendation for new projects. Compared to modern alternatives like React Three Fiber or Framer Motion, React-Famous served a similar niche for 3D and performant animations when those modern tools didn't exist. ([Read more](/details/react-famous.md)) `famo.us` `Bridge` `Rendering`
- [React LocalStorage](https://github.com/STRML/react-localstorage) - Simple componentized localStorage implementation for React. Syncs component state with browser localStorage. ([Read more](/details/react-localstorage.md)) `localStorage` `Persistence` `State Sync`
