## SSR

- [Next.js](https://nextjs.org/) - Widely used React meta-framework that provides server-side rendering, static site generation, file-based routing, API routes, and React Server Components for building production-ready web applications. ([Read more](/details/nextjs.md)) `Meta Framework` `Server Components` `Full Stack`
- [Hypernova](https://github.com/airbnb/hypernova) - Hypernova is Airbnb's open-source microservice for server-side rendering (SSR) JavaScript views, enabling universal rendering through a simple HTTP API that supports multiple JavaScript frameworks simultaneously. It decouples SSR logic from the web server, running a dedicated Node.js service that renders React, Vue, Angular, or vanilla JavaScript components on the server and returns HTML to the client for improved initial page load and SEO. Key features include an HTTP-based SSR API that accepts multiple view configurations in a single request, framework-agnostic architecture supporting React, Vue, Angular, and vanilla JavaScript, built-in fallback rendering that gracefully degrades to client-side rendering if the SSR service is unavailable, error isolation where one failing component doesn't crash the entire page, caching support with server-side memoization to reduce redundant renders, and batch rendering that allows multiple components to be rendered in a single network call. Primary use cases include large-scale web applications requiring improved performance and SEO through server-rendered HTML, microservice architectures where SSR is managed as a separate service, legacy applications incrementally migrating from server-rendered templates to client-side JavaScript, and multi-framework applications where different teams use different JavaScript frameworks. Compared to Next.js or Remix (which integrate SSR at the framework level within a single application), Hypernova offers greater flexibility for multi-framework or legacy architectures through its decoupled microservice approach, though it requires additional infrastructure complexity unlike integrated SSR frameworks. ([Read more](/details/hypernova.md)) `Server Side Rendering` `Airbnb` `Universal`
- [iSSR](https://github.com/AlexSergey/issr) - The easiest way to move your React application to Server-Side Rendering. Handles Side Effects and synchronizes State between server and client. ([Read more](/details/issr.md)) `Server Side Rendering` `Side Effects` `State Sync`
- [Nitro](https://nitro.unjs.io/) - Universal server toolkit for JavaScript that powers Nuxt but works standalone as well. Provides a fast, minimal server engine with support for deploying to multiple platforms including Node.js, serverless, and edge runtimes. ([Read more](/details/nitro.md)) `Server Framework` `Cross Platform` `Unjs`
- [React ESI](https://github.com/dunglas/react-esi) - A library to boost SSR performance by exposing React components as Edge Side Includes (ESI) fragments. Enables partial server-side rendering for improved performance. ([Read more](/details/react-esi.md)) `Server Side Rendering` `ESI` `Performance`
- [React Server](https://github.com/redfin/react-server) - React framework with server rendering for blazing fast page loads. Developed by Redfin, provides isomorphic rendering and progressive enhancement. ([Read more](/details/react-server.md)) `Server Side Rendering` `Progressive Enhancement` `Framework`
- [RedwoodJS](https://redwoodjs.com/) - Full-stack, serverless-ready React framework built on GraphQL. Provides a batteries-included development experience with Prisma for the database, GraphQL for the API layer, Jest for testing, Storybook for component development, and Netlify for deployments. ([Read more](/details/redwoodjs.md)) `Meta Framework` `Graphql` `Full Stack`
- [Rill](https://github.com/rill-js/rill) - Universal web application framework for building isomorphic JavaScript apps with Express-like middleware on both client and server. ([Read more](/details/rill.md)) `Universal` `Isomorphic` `Middleware`
- [TanStack Start](https://tanstack.com/start) - Full-stack React meta-framework built by the TanStack team. Currently in beta, providing type-safe routing, data loading, and React Server Component support while working seamlessly with TanStack Router and TanStack Query. ([Read more](/details/tanstack-start.md)) `Meta Framework` `Type Safe` `TanStack`
- [Waku](https://github.com/dai-shi/waku) - Minimalist React framework with first-class support for React Server Components (RSC). Created by the developer behind Zustand, it provides a lightweight, flexible foundation for modern server-client React applications. ([Read more](/details/waku.md)) `Meta Framework` `Server Components` `Minimalist`

## Testing

- [Enzyme](https://github.com/airbnb/enzyme) - Enzyme is a JavaScript testing utility for React developed by Airbnb that provides intuitive APIs for testing React component output through shallow rendering, full DOM rendering, and static markup analysis. It allows developers to assert, manipulate, and traverse React component trees to verify rendering behavior, state changes, and component interactions in isolation. Key features include shallow rendering for testing components in isolation without child lifecycle methods, full DOM rendering via jsdom with complete component lifecycle execution, static rendered markup for analyzing HTML output, robust selector API supporting CSS selectors and component types, event simulation for user interactions including click, change, and keyboard events, state and prop manipulation for testing conditional rendering paths, and integration with Jest, Mocha, Karma, and other test runners. Primary use cases include unit testing React components to verify render output and props, snapshot testing with rendering manipulation capabilities, integration testing of component interactions with DOM events, and component library testing with prop-based scenario coverage. Note: Enzyme is now in maintenance mode following React 18's rendering changes (concurrent features, automatic batching), and it does not support React 18 natively. For new projects, React Testing Library or Vitest are recommended alternatives. Compared to React Testing Library (which tests from the user perspective rather than implementation details), Enzyme provides deeper access to component internals including state and instance methods, making it better suited for testing component implementation but potentially creating more brittle tests. ([Read more](/details/enzyme.md)) `Testing` `Airbnb` `Assertion`
- [Cypress](https://www.cypress.io/) - Cypress is an end-to-end testing framework designed for modern web applications, running directly in the browser for fast and reliable test execution. It provides an interactive test runner with time-travel debugging, automatic waiting for elements, and network stubbing capabilities. Key features include real-time reloads during test development, automatic screenshots and video recording on failures, component testing for React in isolation, and seamless CI/CD integration. Primary use cases include E2E testing for React SPAs, component testing, integration testing with APIs, and visual regression testing. Compared to Playwright (faster for cross-browser testing, more modern API) and Selenium (more mature but older architecture), Cypress excels in developer experience and debugging capabilities but supports fewer browsers natively. ([Read more](/details/cypress.md)) `E2e` `Testing` `Automation` `Component Testing`
- [Playwright](https://playwright.dev/) - Microsoft's modern end-to-end testing framework for web applications. Enables reliable testing across Chrome, Firefox, and Safari with a single API. Features auto-waiting, web-first assertions, and powerful debugging tools for React applications. ([Read more](/details/playwright.md)) `E2e` `Testing` `Automation` `Cross Browser`
- [React Experiments](https://github.com/HubSpot/react-experiments) - React Experiments is a lightweight A/B testing and feature flag library developed by HubSpot that enables developers to implement controlled UI experiments, variant tests, and progressive feature rollouts directly within React component trees. It offers a simple declarative API for rendering different component variants based on experiment assignments and integrates with analytics platforms for tracking results. Key features include declarative experiment wrapper components, automatic user bucketing and consistent variant assignment across sessions, integration with analytics platforms for metric tracking, support for nested experiments without conflicts, server-side rendering compatibility for SEO-friendly experiment serving, and feature flag toggles for gradual rollouts. Primary use cases include conversion rate optimization experiments, testing UI alternatives before full launch, progressive feature rollouts to user segments, and data-driven design decisions in production React applications. Compared to external A/B testing platforms like Optimizely or VWO (which are heavier and require external scripts), React Experiments provides a lighter, code-native approach integrated directly into the React rendering pipeline. ([Read more](/details/react-experiments.md)) `A B Testing` `Experiments` `Feature Flags`
- [React Unit](https://github.com/pzavolinsky/react-unit) - Lightweight unit test library for ReactJS. Provides simple and fast unit testing utilities for React components without requiring a DOM. ([Read more](/details/react-unit.md)) `Unit Testing` `Lightweight` `No Dom`
- [Unexpected React](https://github.com/bruderstein/unexpected-react) - Plugin for Unexpected to enable testing the full React virtual DOM, and also the shallow renderer. Provides assertion-based testing for React components with rich error messages. ([Read more](/details/unexpected-react.md)) `Testing` `React` `Assertion Library`
- [Vitest](https://vitest.dev/) - A blazing fast unit test framework powered by Vite. Offers Jest-compatible API with native ESM support, TypeScript out of the box, and instant hot module replacement. Perfect for modern React applications using Vite. ([Read more](/details/vitest.md)) `Testing` `Vite` `Unit Tests` `Jest Compatible`

Prevents body scrolling when modals are open while avoiding layout shifts. Essential for accessible, professional modal implementations in React applications. ([Read more](/details/react-remove-scroll.md)) `Scroll` `Modal` `Overlay` `Accessibility`
- [Sentry for React](https://docs.sentry.io/platforms/javascript/guides/react/) - One of the most powerful tools for tracking, debugging, and resolving production issues in React applications with automatic error boundaries and detailed stack traces. ([Read more](/details/sentry-for-react.md)) `Error Tracking` `Monitoring` `Debugging`
- [tailwind-merge](https://github.com/dcastil/tailwind-merge) - A utility function to efficiently merge Tailwind CSS classes, automatically resolving conflicts by keeping only the last class when multiple classes target the same CSS property. ([Read more](/details/tailwind-merge.md)) `Tailwind` `Utilities` `Styling`
- [TanStack Query DevTools](https://tanstack.com/query/latest/docs/framework/react/devtools) - Developer tools for TanStack Query (React Query) allowing visualization and interaction with the query cache, helping debug data fetching in React applications. ([Read more](/details/tanstack-query-devtools.md)) `Devtools` `Debugging` `Query`

Prevents keyboard navigation from leaving a specified container, essential for accessible modals, dropdowns, and overlays. Includes auto-focus and return focus features. ([Read more](/details/react-focus-lock.md)) `Accessibility` `Focus` `Modal` `Keyboard`

Keeps full control over what's rendered. ([Read more](/details/react-headings.md)) `Headings` `Seo` `Accessibility`

## CMS

- [BCMS](https://github.com/bcms/cms) - BCMS is an open-source, self-hostable headless CMS that provides a GraphQL and REST API for managing content across Jamstack frameworks like Gatsby, Next.js, and Nuxt. It decouples content management from frontend rendering, enabling developers to build fast, static sites with dynamic content workflows. Key features include a visual content editor with custom content types, built-in GraphQL and REST APIs, media library management, user role management, multi-language content support, and deployment flexibility (self-hosted or Docker). Primary use cases include Jamstack websites, multi-site content management, marketing sites requiring non-technical content editing, and developer workflows needing programmatic content access. Compared to hosted headless CMS options like Contentful or Strapi Cloud (which are SaaS with usage-based pricing), BCMS offers full data sovereignty with no vendor lock-in since it's self-hosted and open-source. ([Read more](/details/bcms.md)) `Headless` `API-based` `Self Hostable`

## Custom Hooks

- [Ahooks](https://ahooks.js.org) - Ahooks is a high-quality React Hooks library providing 50+ production-ready utilities covering common development scenarios such as state management, side effects, DOM manipulation, and network requests. Developed with a focus on developer experience, it offers comprehensive TypeScript support, SSR compatibility, and detailed documentation with interactive examples.

• 50+ hooks across lifecycle, side effects, DOM, network, and advanced patterns
• useRequest for data fetching with loading, caching, polling, and retry logic
• SSR compatible — all hooks work safely in server-side rendering environments
• Full TypeScript support with auto-generated type definitions

Primary use cases include enterprise React applications, SaaS dashboards, and any project that needs reliable, pre-built hook utilities for common patterns instead of writing custom implementations. Compared to usehooks-ts (smaller, simpler) or React Use (larger but less documented), Ahooks strikes a balance with enterprise-grade reliability, excellent documentation, and a well-organized API surface. ([Read more](/details/ahooks.md)) `Hooks` `Enterprise` `Typescript`
- [React Firebase Hooks](https://github.com/CSFrequency/react-firebase-hooks) - React hooks for Firebase services including Authentication, Firestore, Storage, and Realtime Database. Simplifies Firebase integration with automatic subscription management and loading/error states. TypeScript support included. ([Read more](/details/react-firebase-hooks.md)) `Firebase` `Hooks` `Database` `Authentication`
- [React Hook Mighty Mouse](https://github.com/mkosir/react-hook-mighty-mouse) - A React hook that tracks mouse events on selected elements, providing real-time mouse position and button state data. ([Read more](/details/react-hook-mighty-mouse.md)) `Mouse Tracking` `Custom Hook` `Events`
- [React Use](https://github.com/streamich/react-use) - Comprehensive collection of essential React hooks for common use cases including async operations, side effects, forms, and lifecycle management. Provides battle-tested utilities with full TypeScript support and extensive documentation. ([Read more](/details/react-use.md)) `Hooks` `Utilities` `Open Source`
- [React Waypoint](https://github.com/civiccc/react-waypoint) - Execute a callback when a component enters or leaves the viewport. Perfect for lazy loading, infinite scrolling, animations on scroll, and analytics tracking. Lightweight alternative to Intersection Observer API with React integration. ([Read more](/details/react-waypoint.md)) `Scroll` `Viewport` `Lazy Load` `Infinite Scroll`
- [react-use-measure](https://github.com/pmndrs/react-use-measure) - A React hook for measuring element sizes and positions using ResizeObserver. Provides accurate, performant measurements of DOM elements with support for debouncing and polyfills. Perfect for responsive components and animations. ([Read more](/details/react-use-measure.md)) `Hooks` `Resize` `Observer` `Measurements`
- [react-use-websocket](https://github.com/robtaussig/react-use-websocket) - React Hook for WebSocket communication. Simplifies WebSocket integration in React applications with automatic reconnection, message queuing, and connection state management. Fully typed with TypeScript support. ([Read more](/details/react-use-websocket.md)) `Websocket` `Hooks` `Real Time` `Communication`
- [useCountdown](https://github.com/Mudassar045/react-countdown-hook) - A simple React hook for creating countdown timers. Provides an easy-to-use interface for countdown functionality with pause, resume, and reset capabilities. Perfect for timers, auctions, events, and time-limited offers. ([Read more](/details/usecountdown.md)) `Countdown` `Timer` `Hooks` `Time`
- [usehooks-ts](https://docs.usehooks.ts.org) - usehooks-ts is a modern collection of over 200+ production-ready React hooks that simplify common tasks like form validation, animations, and local storage management. It provides TypeScript support and comprehensive documentation for each hook.
 ([Read more](/details/usehooks-ts.md)) `Custom Hooks` `Typescript` `Productivity`
- [useKeyCapture](https://github.com/pranesh239/use-key-capture) - A custom React hook to ease key-press listeners for target elements or global scope, simplifying keyboard event handling in functional components. ([Read more](/details/usekeycapture.md)) `Custom Hook` `Keyboard` `Event Listeners`

## Data Grid

## Data Management

- [Fireproof](https://github.com/fireproof-storage/fireproof) - Pure JavaScript, zero-dependency CRDT database that runs in the browser and connects to any cloud or backend. Enables real-time collaborative applications with offline support. ([Read more](/details/fireproof.md)) `CRDT` `Local First` `Real Time`
- [RxDB](https://rxdb.info/) - A fast, local-first, reactive Database for JavaScript Applications. Enables offline-first apps with real-time data synchronization across clients. ([Read more](/details/rxdb.md)) `Local First` `Reactive` `Offline First`

## Data Tables & Grids

- [React Virtualized](https://reactvirtualized.github.io/react-virtualized/) - React Virtualized is a pioneering high-performance React component library for efficiently rendering large lists, grids, and tabular data through windowing techniques that only render items visible in the viewport. It supports datasets of hundreds of thousands of rows while maintaining smooth 60fps scrolling and minimal memory usage. Key features include the List, Grid, and Table components for various layout patterns, CellMeasurer for dynamically measuring content dimensions, AutoSizer for responsive container sizing, InfiniteLoader for infinite scroll data fetching, and Collection for rendering irregularly positioned items. Primary use cases include data-heavy admin dashboards, email inbox views, file explorer interfaces, spreadsheet-like data grids, and any application rendering thousands or millions of rows. Compared to newer alternatives like React Window (which offers a simpler, more modern API from the same author), react-virtualized provides more components including Table with built-in column resizing and sorting, though react-window is recommended for new projects due to its smaller API surface and better tree-shaking support. ([Read more](/details/react-virtualized.md)) `Virtualization` `React` `Performance` `Large Lists`

## Real Time Communication

## Rendering Libraries

- [Inferno](https://github.com/infernojs/inferno) - An extremely fast, React-like JavaScript library for building modern user interfaces. Provides a React-compatible API with significantly faster rendering performance. ([Read more](/details/inferno.md)) `React-like` `Performance` `UI-library`
- [React Blessed](https://github.com/Yomguithereal/react-blessed) - React Blessed is a custom React renderer that enables building terminal-based user interfaces using React's declarative component model and the blessed terminal UI library. It translates React's virtual DOM into terminal-compatible output, allowing developers to build CLI tools, dashboards, and terminal apps with familiar React patterns. Key features include full React lifecycle integration with terminal rendering, blessed widget compatibility for terminal UI elements, real-time terminal rendering with reactive state updates, support for terminal key events and mouse input, and seamless use of React hooks within terminal components. Primary use cases include interactive CLI tools, terminal dashboards and monitoring interfaces, system administration tools, and developer tools running in terminal environments. Compared to Ink (a similar React terminal renderer), React Blessed uses blessed's extensive widget ecosystem while Ink focuses on building its own primitive set, making React Blessed better for projects needing rich terminal widgets like lists, tables, and progress bars. ([Read more](/details/react-blessed.md)) `Terminal` `Blessed` `Renderer`

([Read more](/details/plate.md)) `Open Source` `Headless` `Plugin Driven`

Provides inline and block-level formatting including headings, lists, and media support, suitable for content editing interfaces in React applications. ## Starter Kits

- [CRA Template Redux Auth Starter](https://github.com/Nilanth/cra-template-redux-auth-starter) - A Redux authentication starter boilerplate template for Create React App. Provides a foundation for building React applications with Redux-based auth flow, including sign-in, sign-up, and token management. ([Read more](/details/cra-template-redux-auth-starter.md)) `Create React App` `Redux` `Authentication`
- [Create React Dependency](https://github.com/andrelmlins/create-react-dependency) - Create React Dependency is a zero-configuration scaffolding tool that bootstraps reusable React component libraries with minimal setup. It generates a complete project structure with build configuration, testing setup, and publishing workflows, allowing developers to focus on writing components rather than configuring tooling.

**Key Features:**
- Zero build configuration required
- Automated project scaffolding for React component libraries
- Pre-configured bundling with Rollup or similar
- Testing setup included
- Ready for npm publishing

**Primary Use Cases:** Teams creating internal component libraries, open-source React component projects, and developers who want to package React components as standalone npm packages.

**Compared to Alternatives:** Unlike manual setup (configuring Webpack/Rollup, Jest, TypeScript) or create-react-library (more opinionated), this tool offers a minimalist approach with less boilerplate and faster setup time. ([Read more](/details/create-react-dependency.md)) `No Config` `Dependency` `Component Library`
- [Phoenix React Boilerplate](https://github.com/Sazito/phoenix) - A simple React boilerplate with Server Side Rendering and Localization support. Provides a streamlined starting point for building isomorphic React applications with built-in i18n capabilities. ([Read more](/details/phoenix-sazito.md)) `Boilerplate` `Server Side Rendering` `Localization`
- [StarHackIt](https://github.com/FredericHeem/starhackit) - StarHackIt is a full-stack starter kit that provides a complete development environment for building modern web applications with React on the frontend and Node.js on the backend. It includes authentication, database integration, API scaffolding, testing setup, and deployment configuration out of the box.

**Key Features:**
- React frontend with routing and state management
- Node.js/Express backend with REST API scaffolding
- Built-in authentication with JWT tokens
- Database integration with Sequelize ORM
- Testing setup for both frontend and backend
- Docker support for containerized development
- Deployment configuration for multiple cloud platforms

**Primary Use Cases:** Full-stack SaaS applications, MVP prototyping, startup projects requiring rapid development, and teams needing a proven foundation for production-ready web applications.

**Compared to Alternatives:** Unlike create-react-app (frontend-only) or Next.js (focuses on rendering), StarHackIt provides a complete full-stack environment with backend infrastructure. Compared to MEAN/MEVN stacks, it offers more opinionated structure with built-in auth and testing. ([Read more](/details/starhackit.md)) `Full Stack` `Starter Kit` `Scaffolding`

## Text Editors

- [AlloyEditor](https://github.com/liferay/alloy-editor) - AlloyEditor is a modern, free WYSIWYG editor built on top of the CKEditor engine with a completely redesigned UI focused on inline editing simplicity. Originally developed by Liferay, it provides a clean, distraction-free editing toolbar that appears contextually near the user's cursor position, making content creation feel natural and intuitive. Key features include image upload and management, link editing, undo/redo support, full-screen editing mode, and a plugin system for extensibility. Primary use cases include content management systems, blog platforms, and document editing interfaces where a lightweight yet powerful editor is needed. Compared to CKEditor 5's standard UI (which is toolbar-heavy), AlloyEditor's inline approach is cleaner for content-focused applications, though the project has been deprecated and users should consider CKEditor 5 or Tiptap for new projects. ([Read more](/details/alloyeditor.md)) `Wysiwyg` `Ckeditor` `Content Editing`

## Third Party Integrations

- [Auth.js](https://authjs.dev/) - Auth.js (formerly NextAuth.js) is the most popular open-source authentication solution for JavaScript applications, providing session management and authentication with support for 50+ OAuth providers, email magic links, and credential-based login. It offers seamless integration with Next.js and other full-stack frameworks. Key features include support for over 50 OAuth providers (Google, GitHub, Twitter, etc.), email/password and magic link authentication, JWT and database-backed session management, built-in CSRF protection, customizable authentication callbacks, and TypeScript support. Primary use cases include SaaS applications, membership sites, social login integration, and any full-stack web app requiring user authentication. Compared to proprietary solutions like Auth0 (hosted, usage-based pricing) or Clerk (commercial SaaS), Auth.js gives you full control with no vendor lock-in, though it requires self-hosting and managing your own authentication infrastructure. ([Read more](/details/authjs.md)) `Authentication` `Oauth` `Open Source`
- [Braintree](https://www.braintreepayments.com/) - Payment platform acquired by PayPal that provides checkout and payment processing SDKs for React applications. Offers a comprehensive payment solution with support for credit cards, PayPal, Venmo, and other payment methods. ([Read more](/details/braintree.md)) `Payments` `Checkout` `Paypal`
- [Clerk](https://clerk.com/) - Complete user management and authentication platform for React applications. Provides pre-built components for sign up, sign in, user profiles, and session management with enterprise-grade security features. ([Read more](/details/clerk.md)) `Authentication` `User Management` `Saas`
- [Hono](https://hono.dev/) - Ultrafast, lightweight web framework for building APIs and backends that run on any JavaScript runtime including Node.js, Deno, Bun, Cloudflare Workers, and Vercel Edge. A popular choice for React developers who cannot use a full-stack JavaScript framework. ([Read more](/details/hono.md)) `Web Framework` `Edge Runtime` `Typescript`
- [Lemon Squeezy](https://www.lemonsqueezy.com/) - Merchant of record platform built on top of Stripe that handles payments, tax compliance, and subscription management. Provides React integration options for developers who want a simpler alternative to setting up Stripe directly. ([Read more](/details/lemon-squeezy.md)) `Payments` `Subscriptions` `Ecommerce`
- [Lucia Auth](https://lucia-auth.com/) - Lightweight and versatile authentication library for Node.js and JavaScript runtimes. Part of the Lucia ecosystem, providing core authentication primitives, OAuth 2.0 support via Arctic with 50+ providers, and cryptographic utilities via Oslo. ([Read more](/details/lucia-auth.md)) `Authentication` `Oauth` `Lightweight`
- [Mailing](https://www.mailing.run/) - Full-stack email framework for building, testing, and sending transactional emails with React components. Provides local previewing, automated screenshots, and seamless integration for React-based email template workflows. ([Read more](/details/mailing.md)) `Email` `React Components` `Developer Tools`
- [MJML](https://mjml.io/) - Markup language designed to reduce the pain of coding responsive HTML emails. Provides a simple, component-based syntax that compiles to bulletproof responsive email HTML with cross-client compatibility. ([Read more](/details/mjml.md)) `Email` `Responsive` `Markup`
- [PayPal](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/checkout/) - Global payment platform offering seamless integration options for React applications. Provides SDK libraries for processing payments, subscriptions, and checkout flows with a trusted payment experience for end users. ([Read more](/details/paypal.md)) `Payments` `Checkout` `Ecommerce`
- [React Google Analytics](https://github.com/hzdg/react-google-analytics) - Google analytics component for React applications. Provides easy integration with Google Analytics for tracking page views and events. ([Read more](/details/react-google-analytics.md)) `Analytics` `Google Analytics` `Tracking`
- [React Google Analytics Module](https://github.com/react-ga/react-ga) - React Google Analytics Module. Provides a simple way to integrate Google Analytics into React applications with page and event tracking. ([Read more](/details/react-google-analytics-module.md)) `Analytics` `Google Analytics` `Tracking`
- [React Google Autocomplete](https://github.com/ErrorPro/react-google-autocomplete) - Google Places API components and hooks for React. Provides location search with autocomplete powered by Google Places. ([Read more](/details/react-google-autocomplete.md)) `Google Places` `Autocomplete` `Geocoding`
- [React reCAPTCHA](https://github.com/appleboy/react-recaptcha) - A react.js reCAPTCHA component for Google. Provides easy integration of Google reCAPTCHA for bot protection in React applications. ([Read more](/details/react-recaptcha.md)) `Captcha` `Google Recaptcha` `Bot Protection`
- [React Slack Notification](https://github.com/Nilanth/react-slack-notification) - Send messages and error logs to a Slack channel directly from React applications. Provides a simple component for Slack integration. ([Read more](/details/react-slack-notification.md)) `Slack` `Notifications` `Error Logging`
- [React Stripe Checkout](https://github.com/azmenak/react-stripe-checkout) - Load Stripe's checkout.js as a React component. The easiest way to integrate Stripe checkout with React applications. ([Read more](/details/react-stripe-checkout.md)) `Payments` `Stripe` `Checkout`
- [Relay](https://relay.dev/) - Facebook's powerful GraphQL client built for performance and scalability at scale. Provides a data-fetching and caching layer with sophisticated features like data normalization, garbage collection, and automatic query optimization for large React applications. ([Read more](/details/relay.md)) `Graphql` `Data Fetching` `Enterprise`
- [Resend](https://resend.com/) - Email API for developers that enables sending transactional and marketing emails at scale. Provides a React-compatible SDK with excellent deliverability and built-in support for React Email templates. ([Read more](/details/resend.md)) `Email` `Api` `Transactional`
- [Socket.IO Client](https://socket.io) - JavaScript library enabling bi-directional real-time communication between React applications and servers via WebSocket connections with automatic fallback to long polling. Widely used for building live notification systems, chat applications, and collaborative features that require instant updates. ([Read more](/details/socketio-client.md)) `Real Time` `Websocket` `Notifications`
- [tRPC](https://trpc.io/) - End-to-end typesafe API framework for TypeScript applications. Enables calling backend functions directly from the frontend with full type inference, eliminating the need for manual API schema definitions when both frontend and backend share TypeScript. ([Read more](/details/trpc.md)) `Type Safe` `Typescript` `Api`
- [urql](https://formidable.com/open-source/urql/) - Lightweight, highly customizable GraphQL client for React. Developed by Formidable as a performance-focused alternative to Apollo Client, with a simple API and excellent developer experience for consuming GraphQL APIs. ([Read more](/details/urql.md)) `Graphql` `Lightweight` `Client`
- [Web Push](https://github.com/web-push-libs/web-push) - Node.js library implementing the web push protocol for server-side push notification delivery to browsers. Essential for Progressive Web Apps and applications requiring notifications when the app is not actively open, with VAPID key support for secure identification. ([Read more](/details/web-push.md)) `Push Notifications` `Pwa` `Server Side`

Provides mobile-friendly components with gesture support and native-like look and feel. ([Read more](/details/onsen-ui.md)) `Mobile` `Cross Platform` `Hybrid Apps`
- [Park UI](https://park-ui.com/) - Modern React component library built on Ark UI and Panda CSS, released in 2024. Supports React, Vue, Solid.js, and metaframeworks like Next.js and Nuxt with theme editor and pre-built UI blocks. ([Read more](/details/park-ui.md)) `Multi Framework` `Panda Css` `Modern`
- [Preline UI](https://preline.co) - Open-source component library based on Tailwind CSS, offering UI components, blocks, templates, and a Figma design system. Supports React, HTML, Vue, and frameworks like Astro. ([Read more](/details/preline-ui.md)) `Open Source` `Tailwind Css` `Multi Framework`

([Read more](/details/prime-react.md)) `Open Source` `Enterprise` `Primefaces`
- [shadcn-ui](https://github.com/shadcn-ui/ui) - shadcn/ui is a collection of beautifully designed, accessible React components built with Radix UI primitives and Tailwind CSS that can be copied and pasted directly into projects. Rather than a traditional npm dependency, it works as a code registry where developers install and own the component code. Key features include: fully accessible components powered by Radix UI, customizable through Tailwind CSS utility classes, a robust theming system via CSS variables, and comprehensive component coverage for common UI patterns. Primary use cases are building modern web applications, dashboards, SaaS products, and design systems that need a polished, consistent UI. Compared to Material UI (which is heavier and more opinionated) or traditional component libraries, shadcn/ui gives developers full ownership of their component code with zero runtime dependencies and seamless integration into any React/Next.js project. ([Read more](/details/shadcn-ui.md)) `Open Source` `Tailwind Css` `Radix Ui`
- [Tailark](https://tailark.com/) - Beautifully designed collection of marketing UI blocks and templates built on top of shadcn/ui. Delivers high-quality, modern website components with a strong focus on design for marketing websites. ([Read more](/details/tailark.md)) `Marketing` `Shadcn Ui` `Tailwind`
- [tailframes-react-components](https://github.com/Tailframes/react-components) - Open-source React components styled with Tailwind CSS for building responsive and modern web interfaces. Includes 40+ pre-designed UI elements. ([Read more](/details/tailframes-react-components.md)) `Open Source` `Tailwind Css` `React Components`
- [Tailwind UI](https://tailwindui.com/) - Official UI library by the creators of Tailwind CSS providing pre-built, customizable, and production-ready UI components. Offers dozens of pre-designed components with React, Vue, and AlpineJS support. ([Read more](/details/tailwind-ui.md)) `Tailwind` `Premium` `Pre Built Components`
- [untitled-ui-react](https://www.untitledui.com/react) - Open-source React UI component library built with Tailwind CSS and React Aria, offering a comprehensive collection of pre-designed components for rapid development. ([Read more](/details/untitled-ui-react.md)) `Open Source` `Tailwind Css` `React Aria`

## UI Layout

- [AutoResponsive React](https://github.com/xudafeng/autoresponsive-react) - AutoResponsive React is a flexible grid layout library that automatically calculates and positions items within a container based on available width, creating optimal packing layouts without requiring manual breakpoint or column configuration. It uses a packing algorithm to dynamically arrange items of varying heights and widths, making it ideal for masonry-style and asymmetric grid layouts. Key features include automatic responsive reflow on resize, zero-config item packing, support for variable-height items, configurable grid width/height ratios, and touch-friendly transitions. Primary use cases include image galleries, product catalogs, portfolio layouts, dashboard widget grids, and any application needing adaptive grid behavior without media queries. Compared to CSS Grid or Flexbox (which require manual breakpoint definitions), AutoResponsive handles the layout math automatically. ([Read more](/details/autoresponsive-react.md)) `Grid` `Responsive` `Layout`
- [Re-Flex](https://github.com/leefsmp/Re-Flex) - Reflex is a flex layout container component for advanced React web applications, offering resizable panels with high performance and smooth rendering. ([Read more](/details/re-flex.md)) `Flex Layout` `Resizable` `Splitter`
- [React Masonry Component](https://github.com/eiriklv/react-masonry-component) - Wrapper for @desandro's Masonry layout plugin, bringing the popular masonry grid layout pattern to React applications. ([Read more](/details/react-masonry-component.md)) `Masonry` `Grid Layout` `Wrapper`
- [React Spaces](https://github.com/aeagle/react-spaces) - A set of nestable anchored, resizable and scrollable space components that allow building complex UI layouts in a natural and declarative way. ([Read more](/details/react-spaces.md)) `Layout Containers` `Resizable` `Nestable`
- [React Stonecutter](https://github.com/dantrain/react-stonecutter) - Animated grid layout component for React that allows items of varying sizes to flow and reflow with smooth animation transitions. ([Read more](/details/react-stonecutter.md)) `Animated` `Grid Layout` `Masonry`
